# UAD Version History & Release Notes


### Important UAD Software Notes

- Please view the latest <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/210208926" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">macOS & Windows compatibility information</a>.
- macOS requires <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/210208926" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">manual configuration steps</a> to enable UAD software.
- Windows requires <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/27247945568788" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">specific OS settings</a> for optimum UAD performance.
- Always update <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/26454031439892" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">UA device firmware</a> when prompted by UAD software.

### <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/downloads/uad" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Download Latest UAD Software Now</a>

## UAD DSP Software Version 11.8.3 — March 3, 2026

### New

- Apollo x16D Dante Domain Manager/Dante Director support (firmware update required)

### Improved

- (Windows) Apollo driver stability improvements 
- (Windows) Resolved Apollo Solo USB issue preventing AUX routings to DAW
- (Mac) High resolution Retina display graphics for UAD Trident A-Range EQ
- (Mac) High resolution Retina display graphics for UAD Little Labs VOG

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 11.8.2 (Supplemental update for Windows) — December 4, 2025

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### Improved

- (Windows) Resolved issue that could prevent UAD AAX plug-ins from loading in Pro Tools

 

</div>

<div class="accordion__item">

<div class="accordion__item-title">

 

\
Version 11.8.2 — November 18, 2025

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### New

- <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/products/spl-vitalizer-mk3-t" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><strong>UAD SPL Vitalizer MK3-T plug-in</strong></a> for Apollo and UAD-2
- <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/products/elysia-alpha-compressor-v2" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><strong>UAD elysia alpha compressor V2 plug-in</strong></a> for Apollo and UAD-2

### Improved

- (Mac) High resolution Retina display graphics for UAD Ocean Way Studios
- (Windows) Resolved installation warning with recent Dante Controller updates 
- Resolved issue preventing Auto-Tune Realtime plug-in from opening in some applications
- (Apollo UAD Console) Resolved a Monitor Source metering issue with Apollo desktop models

 

</div>

</div>

<div class="accordion__item">

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 11.8.1 — September 4, 2025

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### New

- <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/products/maag-eq4-ms" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Maag EQ4 MS</a> plug-in by Brainworx
- <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/products/shadow-hills-mastering-compressor-class-a" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Shadow Hills Mastering Compressor Class A</a> plug-in by Brainworx
- MIDI Learn for UAD DSP plug-ins

### Improved

- Improved support for touch automation with various UAD plug-ins
- Improved stability with certain Apollo mult-unit configurations
- Console Recall plug-in now displays properly in Pro Tools 2025.6
- Fixed plug-in scanning issues with Ableton Live and Pro Tools 2025.6
- Fixed Apollo Bass Management issues at 176.4 kHz and 196 kHz sample rates
- Fixed issues with Apollo Solo USB driver latency reporting

</div>

</div>

<div class="accordion__item">

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 11.7.1 — June 10, 2025

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### Improved

- Fixed issue saving Apollo line input reference levels
- Fixed issue accessing Apollo Twin inputs at 88.2 kHz and 96 kHz sample rates\
  \
   

</div>

<div class="accordion__item">

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 11.7.0 — May 20, 2025

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### New

- <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/products/a-type-multiband-dynamic-enhancer" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">A-Type Multiband Dynamic Enhancer</a> plug-in for Apollo and UAD-2
- Support for new <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/pages/apollo" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Apollo E Series with Dante</a>
- Support for <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/26387489275412" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">UAD Console v1.2.3</a>
- Support for <a href="360041532452-LUNA-Release-Notes.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">LUNA v1.8.5</a>

### Improved

- (Apollo) Fixed save / recall issues when using Plug-In Scenes with channel strip presets
- Improvements to plug-in resizing

</div>

</div>

<div class="accordion__item">

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 11.6.0 — April 1, 2025

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### Apollo X Series and Apollo X Series Gen 2 Improvements

- All speaker utilities are now available for desktop models
- Mute/solo/trim and metering features are now available for subwoofer output
- Apollo x16D clocking improvements in multi-unit configurations

### Compatibility Changes

- Support for **newest DAWs**
  - **LUNA 1.8**
  - **Logic Pro 11.1**
  - **Ableton Live 12.1**
  - **Cubase 14**
  - **Pro Tools 2024.10**
- macOS **Big Sur 11**, **Monterey 12**, **Ventura 13**, **Sonoma 14**, and **Sequoia 15** are <a href="210208926-Latest-macOS-Windows-Operating-System-Compatibility-Information.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><strong>compatible</strong></a>
- **Windows 10** and **11** are <a href="210208926-Latest-macOS-Windows-Operating-System-Compatibility-Information.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><strong>compatible</strong></a>
- <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/33132923880340-FireWire-Product-Compatibility" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><strong>FireWire</strong></a> connections to Apollo and UAD-2 Satellite are no longer compatible

### Other Changes

- Support for new <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/26387489275412" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank"><strong>UAD Console v1.2.2 features</strong></a>
  - New browser for plug-ins and channel presets
  - New speaker utilities options
  - New open session progress bar
  - New show/hide faders option
  - New sub output meter when bass management enabled in stereo mode
  - Apollo cue output assignments are now saved automatically
  - Various minor fixes and improvements

</div>

</div>

<div class="accordion__item">

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 11.5.2 — December 3, 2024

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### Apollo Monitor Correction Improvements

-  
  - Monitor correction is no longer disabled unexpectedly
  - Bass Management settings are retained after powering off/on
  - Front panel monitor meters now display correct levels under all conditions

</div>

</div>

<div class="accordion__item">

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 11.5.1 — November 12, 2024

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### New in this release

- <span id="h_01J99KCEKBV6GXNYRB0W13JR92">(Apollo X Series) Apollo Monitor Correction by Sonarworks®</span>
- Get Apollo, UAD Console, and UAD-2 updates in **UA Connect**

### Other Changes

- (Apollo X Rack) Fixed various Surround, Bass Management, and ALT monitoring issues

</div>

</div>

<div class="accordion__item">

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 11.5.0 — October 8, 2024

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### New in this release

- Support for new <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/audio-interfaces/apollo.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Apollo X Gen 2 Thunderbolt Audio Interfaces</a>
- <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/audio-interfaces/apollo.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Auto-Gain</a> for Apollo X Gen 2 interface preamps
- <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/audio-interfaces/apollo.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Bass Management</a> for all Apollo X Series interfaces
- Get Apollo, UAD Console, and UAD-2 updates in <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/downloads/uad" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">UA Connect</a>

### Other Changes

- Console Recall plug-in is again available in Pro Tools
- (Apollo Mac) Fixed kernel panic that could occur when changing sample rates
- (Twin X USB) ADAT inputs are no longer offset by two channels
- (Apollo x16D Mac) Minor bug fixes and enhancements
- (Apple Silicon) Fixed playback issue when system awakened from sleep
- (Mac) Fixed installer issue when incorrect password entered on some systems

</div>

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 11.0.1 — December 20, 2023

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### Changes in this Release

- (FireWire) Resolved connectivity issue with Apollo interfaces
- (VST3/AU) Plug-in settings saved with earlier versions now load under all conditions
- (macOS) Improved Apollo sleep compatibility with Apple silicon systems

</div>

</div>

<div class="accordion__item">

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 11.0.0 — November 7, 2023

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### New Features

**Important**: VST3 in UAD 11 brings many new benefits to UAD plug-ins. Note that DAW sessions and UAD presets created or saved with UAD v11 may not load in earlier UAD software. For optimum results, make sure sessions shared between computers are all running the same version. <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/20470221524628" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">See this KB article for details</a>.

- VST3 Support
- New and improved preset browser
- Compatibility with macOS Sonoma

### New Plug-In from Universal Audio

- [Hemisphere Mic Collection](https://www.uaudio.com/hemisphere-microphone-modeling.html) for UA Standard Series microphones

### New Plug-In from Direct Development Partner

- [C-Suite C-Max Limiter](https://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/compressors-limiters/c-suite-c-max-limiter.html) by C-Suite

### Other Changes

- (Console) Fixed various connection and responsiveness issues
- (Console) Fixed offline inputs after editing I/O Matrix and restarting
- (Apollo x4) Fixed multi-unit audio input dropouts after firmware update
- (Brigade) Toggling Vibrato/Chorus now works under all conditions
- (maOS) Resolved several issues with Sonoma operating system
- Various other bug fixes and improvements
- LiveTrack mode has been removed. LiveTrack mode is only available in UAD Software v10.2.5 and earlier.

</div>

</div>

### New Features

<div class="accordion__item-content">

- (Apollo x16) ALT monitoring is now available in all surround and immersive monitor modes

### Other Changes

- (Apollo) Resolved an issue causing Console’s monitor controls to be hidden
- (Apollo Twin X, Apollo x4) Resolved ADAT audio artifacts under rare conditions
- (Apollo x16) Cue 3 can now be mirrored to line outputs

<div class="accordion__item">

Version 10.2.3 — March 21, 2023

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### New Features

- (Apollo x16) New 16-channel immersive audio monitoring support for Dolby Atmos, Auro-3D, and Sony 360 Reality Audio
- (Console) New large resizable Console Output Meters popout window
- (Mac) High resolution Retina display graphics for Cooper Time Cube MkII delay

### Other Changes

- (UAD-2) Resolved offline authorization issues
- (Hitsville Chambers) Improved load times
- (MDWEQ) Resolved key press issue on Apple silicon systems
- (Hitsville EQ Mastering) Mid/Side switch position no longer locked in mono instances
- (Console) Resolved rare issue causing unsaved changes under macOS Ventura
- Various minor fixes and improvements

</div>

Version 10.1.1 — September 13, 2022

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### Changes in this Release

- (Logic) UAD-2 plug-ins are now listed within Logic Pro categories
- (Console) UAD-2 plug-in categories in Console have been updated
- (Console) Keyboard shortcuts now usable when any plug-in window is open
- (Pultec EQs) Stepped control values are now clickable
- (Pultec EQs) Preset copy/paste compatibility with UADx versions
- (Softube) Fixed an issue where settings were not recalled correctly
- (C-Suite C-Vox) Fixed an issue that could cause distortion in Console at high sample rates

- UAD-2 plug-ins are grouped by category in VST DAWs
- Native Apple Silicon support for UAD-2 DSP plug-ins and Apollo Console
- Flex Routes are increased from eight to 16 with Apollo X Series rack models
- New Mix control for Teletronix LA-2A Collection
- (Mac) High resolution Retina display graphics for Teletronix LA-2A Collection

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### Changes in this Release

- (Fender ‘55 Deluxe) Resolved issues with plug-in loading

<div class="accordion__item">

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 9.15.0 — November 9, 2021

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### New UAD Plug-In from Universal Audio

- [Manley Reference Microphone Preamplifier](https://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/channel-strips/manley-reference-microphone-preamplifier.html) with Unison technology

### New UAD Plug-In from Direct Development Partner

- [AMS DMX 15-80 S Digital Delay & Pitch Shifter](https://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/delay-modulation/ams-dmx-digital-delay-pitch-shifter.html) by AMS Neve

### Other Changes

- Apple Silicon M1 Rosetta compatibility
- 32-bit plug-ins are no longer supported
- Many minor bug fixes and improvements
- (UAD) Resolved “Installation Failed” issue during UAD install
- (UAD) Improved metering accuracy with Headroom adjustments on certain plug-ins
- (Galaxy Tape Echo) Resolved crash when dragging Head Select in tempo sync mode
- (API) Improved Mic/Line gain control behaviors
- (H910) Left/right arrow keys now increment/decrement values as expected
- (Capitol Chambers / Ocean Way Studios) Resolved intermittent -38 error
- (Apollo) Fixed duplicated output meters on Apollo Expander Units when unassigned
- (Apollo) Fixed multiple instances of “UA Mixer Engine” in macOS Login Items
- (Apollo x16) Resolved Flex Route Mirror to Monitor issue with certain plug-ins on linked channels
- (Console) Monitor knob no longer jumps to max when clicking text label below control
- (Console) Audio properly passes if plug-in demo not started when Record FX is enabled
- (Big Sur) Fixed blank GUIs for various Softube AU plug-ins in Logic 10.6
- (Big Sur) Resolved crash when inserting RealVerb or DreamVerb
- (Big Sur) Cabinet/recording chain display is no longer degraded with Ampeg bass amps
- (Big Sur) Session name is no longer incorrect when loading session via Console Recall
- (Big Sur) AMS RMX16 buttons are no longer slow to animate
- (Mac) Single installer for supported macOS versions
- (Mac) Apollo FireWire software is now an optional install package
- (Mac) High resolution Retina display graphics for select UAD plug-ins: Bermuda Triangle, Chandler Curve Bender, Chandler Zener Limiter, Dytronics Cyclosonic Panner, Dytronics Tri-Stereo Chorus, Eden WT800, Galaxy Tape Echo, Ibanez Tube Screamer, Marshall Bluesbreaker, Marshall JMP, Marshall Plexi, Marshall Plexi Classic, Marshall Silver Jubilee, OTO Biscuit, Precision Mix Rack Series, Pure Plate Reverb, Raw Distortion, Summit Audio TLA-100A, Tonelux Tilt, TS Overdrive, UA 610-A, UA 610-B.

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 9.14 — May 11, 2021

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### New UAD Plug-Ins from Universal Audio

- [API Vision Channel Strip Collection](https://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/channel-strips/api-vision-channel-strip-collection.html) with Unison technology
  - New API Vision Channel Strip
  - Updated API Vision Channel Strip Legacy
- [API Preamp](https://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/api-preamp.html) with Unison technology

### New UAD Plug-Ins from Direct Development Partner

- [C-Suite C-Vox](https://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/special-processing/c-vox-noise-reduction.html) Noise & Ambience Reduction from C-Suite Audio

### Other Enhancements and Changes

- Refreshed [dbx 160](https://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/compressors-limiters/dbx-160.html) Compressor/Limiter
  - New larger graphic interface
  - New sidechain filter control
  - New parallel Mix control
- (Apollo) Support for LUNA Recording System v1.1.8
- (API 560) Reduced plug-in latency from 56 samples to 55 samples
- (API 2500) Updated default Threshold setting
- (Softube Vocoder) Swipe across band sliders to draw an amplitude curve
- (Softube Vocoder) Resolved intermittent Device Error -38
- (Big Sur) Resolved intermittent issues connecting to UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt
- (Console Recall) Resolved crash that could occur in mono with Pro Tools & macOS Big Sur
- (Apollo) Firmware updates for some models to improve general quality and performance
- (Apollo-Mac) Audio is now sample-aligned when different models are multi-unit cascaded
- (Apollo-Win) Channel Settings are no longer reset when connecting USB models
- (macOS) High resolution Retina display graphics for select UAD plug-ins:
  - Brigade Chorus
  - dbx 160 Compressor
  - Fairchild Tube Limiter Collection
  - Galaxy Tape Echo
  - Precision K-Stereo
  - Studio D Chorus

About this Software

- UAD v9.14.1 is compatible with macOS 11 Big Sur only. Note that UA FireWire products are incompatible with Big Sur.
- UAD v9.14.0 is compatible with Windows and earlier macOS versions.

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 9.13.0 — November 10, 2020

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### New UAD Plug-ins from Universal Audio

- [Neve® Dynamics Collection](https://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/compressors-limiters/neve-dynamics-collection.html)
  - New Neve 2254/E and 2254/E Dual
  - Updated Neve 33609/C and 33609/SE
- Updated [UA 1176 Classic Limiter Collection](https://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/compressors-limiters/1176-collection.html)
  - New Mix, Headroom, and Sidechain filter features
  - High resolution graphics for macOS Retina displays

### Other Enhancements and Changes

- (Townsend Labs Sphere) Four new classic microphone models
- (Console) Resolved issue where channels could remain muted when option-clicking Solo buttons
- (Console) Improved legibility of certain UAD plug-in names
- (Apollo) Resolved playback issue when more than eight LUNA tracks are in ARM
- (Apollo) Monitor Output Gain setting now remains persistent when power-cycling multiple Apollo units
- (Apollo Twin, Apollo Solo) Monitor Bypass is now correctly released after device order change
- (Apollo Twin USB, Apollo Solo) Input type now remains persistent when changing sample rates
- (Satellite USB) Resolved case where device could repeatedly connect/disconnect with certain systems
- (Massenburg DesignWorks EQ) Resolved crash that could occur on some macOS systems
- (Auto-Tune Realtime Advanced) Fixed graphical display issue that could occur on non-retina displays
- (Moog Multimode Filter XL) Settings are now correctly preserved when using ARM in LUNA
- (API Vision Channel Strip) Resolved distortion that could occur when in Auxes in Apollo Console
- (macOS) Resolved issue that could cause delay in responsiveness of Mojave 10.14.6 at startup

- (Console) Pressing spacebar with Console application in foreground now starts/stops the LUNA transport
- (Console) Resolved crash issues with Remove All command and shift-dragging plug-ins

  - UAD API 560
  - UAD API 550A
  - UAD AKG BX20
  - UAD Manley Massive Passive
  - UAD Manley Massive Passive Mastering

### About This Software

- This software is compatible with all UA Audio Interface and UAD-2 products (Arrow, Apollo, Satellite, PCIe) and external connection types (Thunderbolt, FireWire, USB 3).

### Using UAD Plug-Ins with Pro Tools on Windows

Important: After installing UAD software on Windows systems, Pro Tools will display an error the first time the program is launched. Follow the steps below to ensure all UAD plug-ins are ready for use:

Note: These steps are not required when running Windows 10 May 2019 Update (version 1903) or higher.

1.  When Pro Tools is first launched, click "No" when Pro Tools displays a message indicating some UAD AAX plug-ins failed to load. This message can be safely dismissed.
2.  After Pro Tools finishes loading, QUIT Pro Tools. The UAD plug-ins are now ready for use the next time Pro Tools is opened.

Version 9.10.0 — August 6, 2019

<div class="accordion__item-content">

### New UAD Plug-Ins from Universal Audio

- <a href="https://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/compressors-limiters/ua-tube-compressor-collection.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">UA 175B and 176 Tube Compressor Collection</a>

### New Apollo Features

- Channel DSP Pairing for bigger plug-in chains on Console inputs
- +12 dB fader gain for extended mixing range on Console inputs

### Other Enhancements and Changes

UAD Plug-Ins

- (Lexicon 480L) Plug-in latency is significantly reduced
- (Lexicon 480L) Hovering over utility buttons & fader caps shows details in General Info Display
- (Lexicon 480L) Program and Bank now function as discrete parameters
- (Neve 88RS) Pulled knobs appear in correct position when plug-in window is re-opened

- (Townsend Labs Sphere) 10 new microphone models
- (Windows 10) UAD plug-ins now scan correctly on first launch of Pro Tools AAX (requires Win10 v1903)

Apollo and Console

- (Apollo/Arrow) Corrected DSP allocations for UA Audio Interfaces
- (Console) Doubling-clicking Channel label no longer edits adjacent channel
- (Console) Cue Bus Count remains correctly set after session load
- (Console) Aux 2 cue faders are now adjusted as expected when Analog 1 & 2 channels are linked
- (Console) Channel Strip presets saved without a Unison plug-in now recall correctly
- (Console) I/O Matrix no longer shows inactive digital channels as active
- (Twin MkII) Front panel preamp parameters no longer effect Monitor parameters
- (Twin MkII) DIM correctly engages when talkback is pressed
- (Twin USB) Tone no longer occurs if the USB cable is suddenly unplugged
- (Rack models) Digital mirror setting is retained after standalone power cycle
- (Rack models) Input Reference Level is correctly set for both channels when linked
- (Apollo X, Twin MkII) Fixed noise when engaging/disengaging talkback mic from Console
- (Apollo X, Twin MkII) Fixed noise when switching to ADAT input
- (Apollo X) Fixed noise when swapping Monitor units if multiple units connected and audio is streaming
- (Mac) Fixed intermittent crash after sleep/wake if multiple UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt units connected

### About This Software

- Important: macOS Mojave and High Sierra require manual steps to enable UAD software. For details, <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/360016096271" target="_self">see this article</a>.
- This software is compatible with all UA Audio Interface and UAD-2 products (Arrow, Apollo, Satellite, PCIe) and external connection types (Thunderbolt, FireWire, USB 3).
- Apollo Channel DSP Pairing allows bigger UAD plug-in chains on Console inputs by allocating fewer Virtual Channels. By default, fewer Virtual Channels are visible. To view previously-visible Virtual Channels (including original plug-ins and settings), increase the VIRTUAL CHANNELS value in Console Settings\>Hardware Panel\>Channel DSP Pairing. For details, <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/360031316612" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">see this article</a>.
- To learn more about Apollo Channel DSP Pairing, see[Managing DSP Resources](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/360030068452).
- For the latest Mac and Windows OS compatibility information, [see this article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/210208926).
- Corrected DSP allocations for UA Audio Interfaces: – UAD DSP loads are now properly allocated with all Apollo and Arrow interface models. In UAD v9.9 and earlier versions, UAD DSP loads were under-allocated with these models which could result in unreported DSP overloads and audio artifacts. – When Apollo/Arrow sessions that were saved with UAD 9.9 (and lower) are subsequently opened in UAD v9.10 (and higher), the session may report higher UAD loads. If the prior session exceeds the corrected DSP allocations, the "DSP exceeded" dialog appears and any UAD plug-ins that cannot load are disabled. For related information,see[Managing DSP Resources](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/360030068452).

### Windows Setup - Required Settings

Specific Windows operating system settings are necessary for optimum performance when using UAD devices. For details, please review the [Windows Setup - Required Settings](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22Windows+Setup+-+Required+Settings%22&commit=Search) article for your specific device model.

### Firmware Update Information

- This release contains a firmware update for all Thunderbolt models to support Apollo Channel DSP Pairing and Console +12 dB faders.
- For optimum performance, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The UAD software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For more information, see the [UAD firmware updates article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22UAD+Firmware+Updates%22).

### Windows Setup - Required Settings

Specific Windows operating system settings are necessary for optimum performance when using UAD devices. For details, please review the [Windows Setup - Required Settings](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22Windows+Setup+-+Required+Settings%22&commit=Search) article for your specific device model.

### Firmware Update Information

- This release includes Apollo X Series firmware updates for surround sound functionality.
- For optimum performance, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The UAD software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For more information, see the [UAD firmware updates article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22UAD+Firmware+Updates%22).

### Using UAD Plug-Ins with Pro Tools on Windows

Important: After installing UAD software on Windows systems, Pro Tools will display an error the first time the program is launched. Follow these steps to ensure all UAD plug-ins are ready for use:

1.  When Pro Tools is first launched, click "No" when Pro Tools displays a message indicating some UAD AAX plug-ins failed to load. This message can be safely dismissed.
2.  After Pro Tools finishes loading, QUIT Pro Tools. The UAD plug-ins are now ready for use the next time Pro Tools is opened.\
     

</div>

</div>

### New Features

**Note:** This software now includes support for Apollo X with the latest generation of Apple Mac Pro computers (Late 2013 “black cylinder” models). For details, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/360015509371-Mac-Pro-Late-2013-compatibility-with-Apollo-X-Series-Interfaces).

### About This Software

- This software is compatible with all UA Audio Interface and UAD-2 products (Apollo, Arrow, Satellite, PCIe) and external connection types (Thunderbolt, FireWire, USB 3).
- Up to four UA Audio Interfaces and six total UAD-2 devices can be combined within the general guidelines below (one UA audio interface connection type per system). For specific details, see the [UA Device Compatibility article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22UA+Device+Compatibility%22) for your particular model.

### macOS

- This software is compatible with macOS 10.10 Yosemite, 10.11 El Capitan, 10.12 Sierra, and 10.13 High Sierra (Apollo X Series and Arrow require Sierra or High Sierra). For the latest OS compatibility information, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/210208926-macOS-10-12-Sierra-Compatibility-Info).
- With High Sierra, UAD software must be explicitly allowed to load in the Security & Privacy pane within macOS System Preferences. For details, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/115004808426-macOS-10-13-High-Sierra-Compatibility-Info).
- Connect up to four UA Thunderbolt audio interfaces (one Apollo Twin and one Arrow maximum).\`
- Connect up to two Apollo FireWire or two Apollo 16 FireWire units.
- UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt, UAD-2 Satellite FireWire, and UAD-2 PCIe cards can be combined with each other and UA audio interfaces (maximum two UAD FireWire devices).
- Apollo Twin USB and UAD-2 Satellite USB are incompatible with Mac systems.

### Windows

- This software is compatible with 64-bit editions of Microsoft Windows 7, Windows 8.1, and Windows 10 (including Windows 10 Anniversary Update and Windows 10 Fall Creators Update). UA Audio Interfaces require Windows 10. For the latest OS compatibility information, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/210208926-macOS-10-12-Sierra-Compatibility-Info).
- Connect up to four UA Thunderbolt audio interfaces (one Apollo Twin and one Arrow maximum) to Thunderbolt 3-equipped Windows 10 PCs (Thunderbolt 3 to Thunderbolt adapter required, except with Apollo X Series and Arrow).
- Connect up to two Apollo FireWire or two Apollo 16 FireWire units to Windows 7, 8.1, or 10 PCs.
- Connect one Apollo Twin USB to Windows 7, 8.1, or 10 PCs.
- UAD-2 Satellite (Thunderbolt, FireWire, USB) and UAD-2 PCIe cards can be combined with each other and UA Thunderbolt, USB, and FireWire audio interfaces (maximum two UAD FireWire devices and two UAD USB devices).

### Windows Setup - Required Settings

Specific Windows operating system settings are necessary for optimum performance when using UAD devices. For details, please review the <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22Windows+Setup+-+Required+Settings%22&commit=Search" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Windows Setup - Required Settings</a> article for your specific device model.

### Firmware Update Information

- For optimum performance, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The UAD software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, review the [UAD firmware updates article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22UAD+Firmware+Updates%22).

### Thunderbolt Mixed Multi-Unit Compatibility with Windows 10 PC Systems

- All Thunderbolt-equipped Apollo, Arrow, and UAD-2 Satellite products are compatible.
- Up to four UA audio interfaces can be combined via Thunderbolt (one Apollo Twin and one Arrow maximum).
- A total of six Thunderbolt-equipped UAD devices can be connected.
- A PC computer featuring Thunderbolt 3 via USB-C is required.
- A qualified Thunderbolt 3 to Thunderbolt adapter is required (not included), except with Arrow.
- Windows 10 with Anniversary Update (64-Bit Edition) is required.
- For complete Windows Thunderbolt compatibility information, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/214427746).

- Connect up to four UA Thunderbolt audio interfaces (one Apollo Twin and one Arrow maximum) to Thunderbolt 3-equipped Windows 10 PCs (Thunderbolt 3 to Thunderbolt adapter required, except with Arrow).
- Connect up to two Apollo FireWire or two Apollo 16 FireWire units to Windows 7, 8.1, or 10 PCs.
- Connect one Apollo Twin USB to Windows 7, 8.1, or 10 PCs.
- UAD-2 Satellite (Thunderbolt, FireWire, USB) and UAD-2 PCIe cards can be combined with each other and UA Thunderbolt, USB, and FireWire audio interfaces (maximum two UAD FireWire devices and two UAD USB devices).

### Thunderbolt Mixed Multi-Unit Compatibility with Windows 10 PC Systems

- All Thunderbolt-equipped Apollo, Arrow, and UAD-2 Satellite products are compatible.
- Up to four UA audio interfaces can be combined via Thunderbolt (one Apollo Twin and one Arrow maximum).
- A total of six Thunderbolt-equipped UAD devices can be connected.
- A PC computer featuring Thunderbolt 3 via USB-C is required.
- A qualified Thunderbolt 3 to Thunderbolt adapter is required (not included), except with Arrow.
- Windows 10 with Anniversary Update (64-Bit Edition) is required.
- For complete Windows Thunderbolt compatibility information, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/214427746).

### Windows Setup - Required Settings

Specific Windows operating system settings are necessary for optimum performance when using UAD devices. For details, please review the <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22Windows+Setup+-+Required+Settings%22&commit=Search" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Windows Setup - Required Settings</a> article for your specific device model.

### Firmware Update Information

- For optimum performance, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The UAD software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, review the [UAD firmware updates article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22UAD+Firmware+Updates%22).

### Using UAD Plug-Ins with Pro Tools on Windows

Important: After installing UAD software on Windows systems, Pro Tools will display an error the first time the program is launched. Follow these steps to ensure all UAD plug-ins are ready for use:

1.  When Pro Tools is first launched, click "No" when Pro Tools displays a message indicating some UAD AAX plug-ins failed to load. This message can be safely dismissed.
2.  After Pro Tools finishes loading, QUIT Pro Tools. The UAD plug-ins are now ready for use the next time Pro Tools is opened.\
     

</div>

</div>

### New Features

- (Thunderbolt) The audio drivers for Apollo and Arrow are renamed to Universal Audio Thunderbolt. If the previous driver name was selected in a DAW, the new driver name may need to be manually selected in the DAW after installing this software.

### About This Software

- This software is compatible with all UAD-2 products (Apollo, Arrow, Satellite, PCIe) and external connection types (Thunderbolt, FireWire, USB 3).
- Up to six UA audio interfaces and/or UAD-2 devices can be combined within the general guidelines below (one UA audio interface connection type per system). For specific details, see the [UA Device Compatibility article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22UA+Device+Compatibility%22) for your particular model.

### macOS

- This software is compatible with macOS 10.10 Yosemite, 10.11 El Capitan, 10.12 Sierra, and 10.13 High Sierra (Arrow requires Sierra or High Sierra). For the latest OS compatibility information, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/210208926-macOS-10-12-Sierra-Compatibility-Info).
- With High Sierra, UAD software must be explicitly allowed to load in the Security & Privacy pane within macOS System Preferences. For details, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/115004808426-macOS-10-13-High-Sierra-Compatibility-Info).
- Connect up to four UA Thunderbolt audio interfaces (one Apollo Twin and one Arrow maximum).\`
- Connect up to two Apollo FireWire or two Apollo 16 FireWire units.
- UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt, UAD-2 Satellite FireWire, and UAD-2 PCIe cards can be combined with each other and UA audio interfaces (maximum two UAD FireWire devices).
- Apollo Twin USB and UAD-2 Satellite USB are incompatible with Mac systems.

### Windows

- This software is compatible with 64-bit editions of Microsoft Windows 7, Windows 8.1, and Windows 10 (including Windows 10 Anniversary Update and Windows 10 Fall Creators Update). For the latest OS compatibility information, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/210208926-macOS-10-12-Sierra-Compatibility-Info).
- Connect up to four UA Thunderbolt audio interfaces (one Apollo Twin and one Arrow maximum) to Thunderbolt 3-equipped Windows 10 PCs (Thunderbolt 3 to Thunderbolt adapter required, except with Arrow).
- Connect up to two Apollo FireWire or two Apollo 16 FireWire units to Windows 7, 8.1, or 10 PCs.
- Connect one Apollo Twin USB to Windows 7, 8.1, or 10 PCs.
- UAD-2 Satellite (Thunderbolt, FireWire, USB) and UAD-2 PCIe cards can be combined with each other and UA Thunderbolt, USB, and FireWire audio interfaces (maximum two UAD FireWire devices and two UAD USB devices).

 

### Thunderbolt Mixed Multi-Unit Compatibility with Windows 10 PC Systems

- All Thunderbolt-equipped Apollo, Arrow, and UAD-2 Satellite products are compatible.
- Up to four UA audio interfaces can be combined via Thunderbolt (one Apollo Twin and one Arrow maximum).
- A total of six Thunderbolt-equipped UAD devices can be connected.
- A PC computer featuring built-in Thunderbolt 3 via USB-C is required.
- A qualified Thunderbolt 3 to Thunderbolt adapter is required (not included), except with Arrow.
- Windows 10 with Anniversary Update (64-Bit Edition) is required.
- For complete Windows Thunderbolt compatibility information, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/214427746).

### Windows Setup - Required Settings

Specific Windows operating system settings are necessary for optimum performance when using UAD devices. For details, please review the <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22Windows+Setup+-+Required+Settings%22&commit=Search" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Windows Setup - Required Settings</a> article for your specific device model.\
\
 

### Firmware Update Information

- This software includes a firmware update for Arrow.
- For optimum performance, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The UAD software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, review the [UAD firmware updates article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22UAD+Firmware+Updates%22).

### Using UAD Plug-Ins with Pro Tools on Windows

Important: After installing UAD software on Windows systems, Pro Tools will display an error the first time the program is launched. Follow these steps to ensure all UAD plug-ins are ready for use:

1.  When Pro Tools is first launched, click "No" when Pro Tools displays a message indicating some UAD AAX plug-ins failed to load. This message can be safely dismissed.
2.  After Pro Tools finishes loading, QUIT Pro Tools. The UAD plug-ins are now ready for use the next time Pro Tools is opened.

- [SSL 4000 E Channel Strip Collection](http://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/channel-strips/ssl-4000-e-series-channel-strip-collection.html) featuring Unison preamp technology
- [Moog Multimode Filter Collection](http://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/special-processing/moog-multimode-filter-xl-collection.html) featuring Moog Multimode Filter XL

###  

### New UAD Plug-Ins from Direct Development Partners

- [OTO BISCUIT 8-bit Effects](http://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/special-processing/uad-oto-biscuit-effects-plug-in.html) by Softube
- [Fuchs® Overdrive Supreme 50 Amplifier](http://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/guitar-bass/fuchs-overdrive-amp-plug-in.html) by Brainworx
- [bx_subsynth Subharmonic Synth](http://www.uaudio.com/uad-plugins/special-processing/brainworx-bx-subsynth.html) by Brainworx

### New Platform Features

- Thunderbolt mixed multi-unit compatibility with Windows 10 systems
- Console 2 software for FireWire multi-unit systems
- Full qualification of macOS Sierra

### Other Enhancements and Changes

- (Win 10) Resolved driver signing issue with new Windows 10 installations
- (Apollo Thunderbolt Win) Resolved ability to select audio driver in some DAWs. Note: The audio driver must be reselected after installing this software.
- (Apollo Thunderbolt Win) Resolved distortion after sample rate change with large buffer sizes
- (Apollo Thunderbolt Win) General improvements with Windows WDM audio
- (Apollo Thunderbolt Mac) Core Audio selection is automatic with Apollo connect/disconnect
- (Apollo Twin MkII) Resolved audio artifacts that could occur in Line 3-4 outputs
- (Apollo Twin MkII) Resolved multi-unit cue outputs issue when Apollo Twin MkII is monitor unit
- (Apollo FireWire) FireWire audio driver enhancements
- (Console 2) MON buttons are relabeled MIX
- (Console 2) Resolved channel strip preset loading via right-click on Unison insert
- (Console 2) Resolved issue when removing offline unit containing Unison plug-in
- (Console 2) Resolved issue preventing key commands from being passed to Cubase
- (Console 2) Resolved various graphic display issues
- (Console 2 Win) Console Settings can now be opened via DAW settings
- (Fairchild 660/670) Resolved VU meter issue in mono instantiations at 4x sample rates
- (Precision Limiter) Resolved audio artifacts that could occur under certain conditions
- (Precision Reflection Engine) Resolved issues when entering out of range text

### Operating System Compatibility

- This software is compatible with 64-bit editions of Microsoft Windows 7, Windows 8.1, and Windows 10, including Windows 10 Anniversary Update.
- This software is compatible with macOS 10.10 Yosemite, 10.11 El Capitan, and 10.12 Sierra.
- Previous OS versions may be compatible, but they are no longer tested or supported. Prior software for older OS versions is available in the <a href="https://help.uahttps//help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/215267203" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">UAD Software Archives</a>.

### Thunderbolt Mixed Multi-Unit Compatibility with Windows 10 PC Systems

- All Thunderbolt-equipped Apollo and UAD-2 Satellite products are compatible.
- Up to four Apollo units can be combined via Thunderbolt (maximum one Apollo Twin).
- A total of six Thunderbolt-equipped UAD devices can be connected.
- A PC computer featuring built-in Thunderbolt 3 via USB-C is required.
- A qualified Thunderbolt 3 to Thunderbolt adapter is required (not included).
- Windows 10 with Anniversary Update (64-Bit Edition) is required.
- For complete Windows Thunderbolt compatibility information, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/214427746).

### Windows Setup - Required Settings

Specific Windows operating system settings are necessary for optimum performance when using UAD devices. For details, please review the <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22Windows+Setup+-+Required+Settings%22&commit=Search" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Windows Setup - Required Settings</a> article for your specific device model.

### Apollo Driver Name (Windows Thunderbolt)

- The Apollo audio driver for Windows Thunderbolt ASIO is renamed in this software. If a previous Apollo driver name was selected in the DAW, the new driver name may need to be manually selected after installing this software.

### Console 2 application for Apollo FireWire multi-unit cascading

- UAD v9.1.0 introduces Console 2 software for multi-unit cascading of two first-generation (silver) Apollo or Apollo 16 models connected via FireWire. For Console 2 operating instructions, see the [Apollo FireWire Software Manual](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/213746106).
- Wiring requirements for FireWire multi-unit cascading are unchanged. For FireWire multi-unit cascading wiring requirements, [see this KB article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/204842196-Apollo-FireWire-Multi-Unit-Cascading).

### Apollo FireWire Driver Improvements

Apollo’s FireWire audio driver has been enhanced for stability and performance. As a result, Apollo audio streams use more FireWire bandwidth versus previous versions. The UAD Bandwidth Allocation setting (in UAD Meter & Control Panel) may need to be reduced to compensate when UAD plug-ins are used within a DAW. Additional FireWire improvements include:

- (Win) ASIO and WDM sample rates are automatically matched
- (Win 10) Advanced panel is accessible at Control Panel\>Sound\>Recording/Playback
- (Mac) Audio playback is no longer distorted with Quicktime 10

### Firmware Update Information

- UAD v9.1 contains a firmware update for Apollo Twin MkII.
- For optimum performance, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, review the [UAD firmware updates article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22UAD+Firmware+Updates%22).

### Using UAD Plug-Ins with Pro Tools on Windows

Important: After installing UAD software on Windows systems, Pro Tools will display an error the first time the program is launched. Follow these steps to ensure all UAD plug-ins are ready for use:

1.  When Pro Tools is first launched, click "No" when Pro Tools displays a message indicating some UAD AAX plug-ins failed to load. This message can be safely dismissed.
2.  After Pro Tools finishes loading, QUIT Pro Tools. The UAD plug-ins are now ready for use the next time Pro Tools is opened.\
     

### Known Issue with earlier UAD Software and macOS Sierra

#### Note: The following issue does NOT occur whenUAD v9.1 (or higher) is installed before upgrading to macOS Sierra.

Symptom: Installing UAD v8.7 or earlier software onto a macOS Sierra system, or upgrading to macOS Sierra with earlier UAD software installed, may cause the system to fail on startup.

Solution: If the computer will not startup, start the computer in Safe mode by holding down the Shift key during startup, then run the Uninstall Universal Audio Software application located in /Applications/Universal Audio. After uninstalling, install [v9.1 (or higher)](http://www.uaudio.com/uad/downloads/), or install/restore a previous version of macOS.\
\
 

</div>

</div>

### Details About This Release

#### Operating System Compatibility

- This software is compatible with 64-bit editions of Microsoft Windows 7, Windows 8.1, and Windows 10, including Windows 10 Anniversary Update.
- This software is compatible with macOS 10.9 Mavericks, 10.10 Yosemite, and 10.11 El Capitan.

For the latest macOS Sierra information,<a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/210208926-macOS-10-12-Sierra-Compatibility-Info" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">review this KB article</a>.

Thunderbolt Compatibility with Windows 10 PC Systems

- All Thunderbolt-equipped Apollo and UAD-2 products are compatible.
- A PC computer featuring built-in Thunderbolt 3 via USB-C is required.
- A qualified Thunderbolt 3 to Thunderbolt adapter is required (not included).
- Windows 10 with Anniversary Update (64-Bit Edition) is required.
- Connecting more than one Apollo via Thunderbolt (multi-unit cascading) is currently incompatible. This feature will be available in Q1 2017.
- For complete compatibility information,<a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/214492726" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">review this KB article</a>.

Windows Setup - Required Settings

- Specific Windows operating system settings are necessary for optimum performance when using UAD devices. For details, please review the[Windows Setup - Required Settings](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22Windows+Setup+-+Required+Settings%22&commit=Search)articlefor your specific device model.

#### Initializing AAX 64 for Windows

Important: To use Avid Pro Tools 11 or Pro Tools 12 with UAD AAX 64 plug-ins under Windows, the following steps are required. This procedure must be performed each time an updated version of UAD software is installed:

1.  Install the latest UAD software. Be sure to restart the computer after installation.
2.  Open the Pro Tools application. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are automatically scanned during launch.
3.  Click "No" when Pro Tools displays a message indicating some UAD AAX plug-ins failed to load. This message can be safely dismissed.
4.  After all plug-in scans are complete, QUIT Pro Tools. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are now properly initialized and ready for use the next time Pro Tools is opened.

#### Changing Apollo FireWire/Thunderbolt Connectivity

- All Apollo FireWire models can be upgraded to Thunderbolt connectivity withthe Thunderbolt Option Card.
- To upgrade an Apollo with FireWire firmware to Thunderbolt connectivity, simply install the Thunderbolt Option Card, connect the unit to a Thunderbolt port, and follow the on-screen instructions.
- Upgrading to Thunderbolt will disable Apollo FireWire ports. However, FireWire devices can still be daisy-chained from Apollo’s second Thunderbolt port using an Apple Thunderbolt to FireWire adapter.
- The UAD Meter & Control Panel application can be used to restore FireWire connectivity to Apollo FireWire models that have been updated with Thunderbolt firmware.
  - To change the Apollo firmware from Thunderbolt to FireWire, select “Revert to FireWire connectivity…” from the UAD Meter Menu, then follow the on-screen instructions.
  - Note: The new menu function only appears when an Apollo or Apollo 16 FireWire unit (silver rack models only) is equipped with the Thunderbolt Option Card, the unit is connected to the computer via Thunderbolt, and Thunderbolt firmware is installed in the unit.

#### Firmware Update Information

- This release contains a firmware update for all Apollo Thunderbolt models.
- For optimum results, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, review the <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%E2%9C%93&query=%22Firmware+Updates%22&commit=Search" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">firmware updates article</a> for your device.\
   

### Known Issue with earlier UAD Software and macOS Sierra

#### Note: The following issue does NOT occur whenUAD v9.0.2 (or higher) is installed before upgrading to macOS Sierra.

Symptom: Installing UAD v8.7 or earlier software onto a macOS Sierra system, or upgrading to macOS Sierra with earlier UAD software installed, may cause the system to fail on startup.

Solution: If the computer will not startup, start the computer in Safe mode by holding down the Shift key during startup, then run the Uninstall Universal Audio Software application located in /Applications/Universal Audio. After uninstalling, install [v9.0.2 (or higher)](http://www.uaudio.com/uad/downloads/), or install/restore a previous version of macOS.\

<div class="accordion__item-title">

Version 8.7.4 and prior versions

</div>

<div class="accordion__item-content">

## Version 8.7.4 - August 16, 2016

### About This Software (Mac only)

- This software is compatible with Apollo audio interfaces using Thunderbolt for the computer connection.
- This software is compatible with UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt, UAD-2 Satellite FireWire, and UAD-2 PCIe cards.
- This software is incompatible with UAD-2 Satellite USB and Apollo Twin USB.

#### Changes In This Release

- (Manley VOXBOX) Resolved issue causing graphic anomalies or unresponsive system under certain conditions

### Details About This Release

#### Firmware Update Information

- For optimum results, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, visit the [firmware updates Knowledge Base article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%C3%A2%C5%93%E2%80%9C&query=%22UAD+Firmware+Updates+%28Mac%29%22&commit=Search).

#### Mac OS X Compatibility

- This software is tested and compatible with Mac OS X 10.9 Mavericks, 10.10 Yosemite, and 10.11 El Capitan.
- Pre-release and beta operating systems are not supported.

#### Apollo Expanded Information

- Multi-Unit Cascading: Inter-unit wiring is changed with UAD v8. Only a single Thunderbolt cable is needed for each Apollo unit, and no other cables (ADAT, Word Clock, FireWire, MADI) should be connected between Apollo units. See the <a href="../../fr.html" target="_self">UA Support Knowledge Base</a> or <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/manuals.html" target="_self">Apollo Thunderbolt Software Manual</a> for details.
- Device Compatibility: For detailed device compatibility information related to UAD v8, visit the <a href="../../fr.html" target="_self">UA Support Knowledge Base</a>.

### About Apollo Thunderbolt Software

- This release uses the PCIe protocol via Thunderbolt for all audio I/O stream processing. Because FireWire I/O drivers are not included, Thunderbolt must be used for Apollo’s connection to the computer.
- Important: Apollo Thunderbolt software disables the FireWire ports on Apollo and Apollo 16. After loading the required firmware contained in all [UAD Thunderbolt software](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html#sw):
  - Apollo cannot be connected to the computer via FireWire
  - FireWire devices cannot be connected to the Apollo FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices must be disconnected from Apollo’s FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices may be connected to different FireWire ports, such as a:
    - FireWire port on the Mac (if available)
    - Thunderbolt port via the <a href="http://www.apple.com/shop/product/MD464LL/A/apple-thunderbolt-to-firewire-adapter" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Apple Thunderbolt to FireWire Adapter</a>
    - Thunderbolt hub that has a FireWire port
- Apollo's firmware can be manually downgraded to reenable FireWire port functionality. For instructions, see the [Mac firmware updates Knowledge Base article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%C3%A2%C5%93%E2%80%9C&query=%22UAD+Firmware+Updates+%28Mac%29%22&commit=Search).

#### Compatibility Requirements, Technical Resources, and Customer Support

- For complete UAD-2 and Apollo system requirements, detailed compatibility information, setup videos, and additional support resources, visit the <a href="../../fr.html" target="_self">UA Support Knowledge Base</a>.

- This software is incompatible with UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt, UAD-2 Satellite USB, Apollo Twin, Apollo Twin USB, and next-gen Apollo models without FireWire ports.

- This software is incompatible with UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt.

### New UAD Plug-Ins from Universal Audio

- [Manley® VOXBOX Channel Strip](http://www.uaudio.com/store/unison/manley-voxbox.html)
- [Brigade Chorus Pedal](http://www.uaudio.com/store/delay-modulation/brigade-chorus.html)

### Other Enhancements

- (Fender 55 Tweed Deluxe) Speaker knob responds to vertical drag in linear control mode
- (Fender 55 Tweed Deluxe) Power switch releases DSP when DSP LoadLock is off
- (Apollo) Console's Unison inserts are now identified by "UNISON +" text overlay
- (bx_digital V3 EQ Collection) Various fixes and improvements
- Improved graphical interfaces and Pro Tools page tables for existing UAD plug-ins: Manley Massive Passive EQ, Manley Massive Passive Mastering EQ
- Usage statistics option helps improve UAD products

### Details About This Release

#### Windows Setup - Required Settings

- Specific Windows operating system settings are necessary for optimum performance when using Apollo Twin USB and UAD-2 Satellite USB. For details, please review the <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/208139723-Windows-Setup-Required-Settings" target="_self">Windows Setup - Required Settings</a>Knowledge Base article.

#### Windows OS compatibility

- This software is tested and compatible with 64-bit editions of Microsoft Windows 7, Windows 8.1, and Windows 10.
- Pre-release and beta operating systems are not supported.

#### Initializing AAX 64 for Windows

- Important: To use Avid Pro Tools 11 or Pro Tools 12 with UAD AAX 64 plug-ins under Windows, the following steps are required. This procedure must be performed each time an updated version of UAD software is installed: 1. Install the [latest UAD software](http://www.uaudio.com/downloads). Be sure to restart the computer after installation. 2. Open the Pro Tools application. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are automatically scanned during launch. 3. Click "No" when Pro Tools displays a message indicating some UAD AAX plug-ins failed to load. This message can be safely dismissed. 4. After all plug-in scans are complete, QUIT Pro Tools. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are now properly initialized and ready for use the next time Pro Tools is opened.

#### Firmware Update Information

- For optimum results, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, visit the [firmware updates Knowledge Base article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%C3%A2%C5%93%E2%80%9C&query=%22UAD+Firmware+Updates+%28Windows%29%22&commit=Search).

## Version 8.7.1 - August 2, 2016

### About This Software (Mac only)

- This software is compatible with Apollo audio interfaces using Thunderbolt for the computer connection.
- This software is compatible with UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt, UAD-2 Satellite FireWire, and UAD-2 PCIe cards.
- This software is incompatible with UAD-2 Satellite USB and Apollo Twin USB.

### New UAD Plug-Ins from Universal Audio

- [Manley® VOXBOX Channel Strip](http://www.uaudio.com/store/unison/manley-voxbox.html)
- [Brigade Chorus Pedal](http://www.uaudio.com/store/delay-modulation/brigade-chorus.html)
- [Galaxy Tape Echo](http://www.uaudio.com/store/delay-modulation/galaxy-tape-echo.html)
- [Studio D Chorus](http://www.uaudio.com/store/delay-modulation/studio-d-chorus.html)

### New UAD Plug-In from Direct Development Partner

- [Ampeg® B-15N Bass Amplifier](http://www.uaudio.com/store/guitar-bass/ampeg-b15n.html) by Brainworx

### Other Enhancements

- (Fender 55 Tweed Deluxe) Speaker knob responds to vertical drag in linear control mode
- (Fender 55 Tweed Deluxe) Power switch releases DSP when DSP LoadLock is off
- (bx_digital V3 EQ Collection) Various fixes and improvements
- (Apollo) Corrected DSP allocations for next-gen Apollo 8/8p/16mkII models
- (Apollo) Console's Unison inserts are now identified by "UNISON +" text overlay
- (Apollo) Core Audio I/O factory presets are available for next-gen Apollo 8/8p/16mkII models
- Improved graphical interfaces and Pro Tools page tables for existing UAD plug-ins: Manley Massive Passive EQ, Manley Massive Passive Mastering EQ
- Usage statistics option helps improve UAD products

### Details About This Release

#### Corrected DSP allocations for next-gen Apollo 8/8p/16mkII models

- UAD DSP loads are now properly allocated with next-generation (black) Apollo 8, Apollo 8p, and Apollo 16 mkII rack models. In UAD v8.6 and earlier versions, UAD DSP loads were under-allocated with these models which could result in unreported DSP overloads and audio artifacts.
- With these Apollo models, when sessions that were saved with UAD v8.6 (and lower) are subsequently opened in UAD v8.7 (and higher), the session may report higher UAD loads. If the prior session exceeds the corrected DSP allocations, a "DSP exceeded" dialog will appear and any UAD plug-ins that cannot load are disabled as originally intended.

### Firmware Update Information

- For optimum results, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, visit the [firmware updates Knowledge Base article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%C3%A2%C5%93%E2%80%9C&query=%22UAD+Firmware+Updates+%28Mac%29%22&commit=Search).

#### Mac OS X Compatibility

- This software is tested and compatible with Mac OS X 10.9 Mavericks, 10.10 Yosemite, and 10.11 El Capitan.
- Pre-release and beta operating systems are not supported.

#### Apollo Expanded Information

- Multi-Unit Cascading: Inter-unit wiring is changed with UAD v8. Only a single Thunderbolt cable is needed for each Apollo unit, and no other cables (ADAT, Word Clock, FireWire, MADI) should be connected between Apollo units. See the <a href="../../fr.html" target="_self">UA Support Knowledge Base</a> or <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/manuals.html" target="_self">Apollo Thunderbolt Software Manual</a> for details.
- Device Compatibility: For detailed device compatibility information related to UAD v8, visit the <a href="../../fr.html" target="_self">UA Support Knowledge Base</a>.

### About Apollo Thunderbolt Software

- This release uses the PCIe protocol via Thunderbolt for all audio I/O stream processing. Because FireWire I/O drivers are not included, Thunderbolt must be used for Apollo’s connection to the computer.
- Important: Apollo Thunderbolt software disables the FireWire ports on Apollo and Apollo 16. After loading the required firmware contained in all [UAD Thunderbolt software](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html#sw):
  - Apollo cannot be connected to the computer via FireWire
  - FireWire devices cannot be connected to the Apollo FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices must be disconnected from Apollo’s FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices may be connected to different FireWire ports, such as a:
    - FireWire port on the Mac (if available)
    - Thunderbolt port via the <a href="http://www.apple.com/shop/product/MD464LL/A/apple-thunderbolt-to-firewire-adapter" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Apple Thunderbolt to FireWire Adapter</a>
    - Thunderbolt hub that has a FireWire port
- Apollo's firmware can be manually downgraded to reenable FireWire port functionality. For instructions, see the [Mac firmware updates Knowledge Base article](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/search?utf8=%C3%A2%C5%93%E2%80%9C&query=%22UAD+Firmware+Updates+%28Mac%29%22&commit=Search).

#### Compatibility Requirements, Technical Resources, and Customer Support

- For complete UAD-2 and Apollo system requirements, detailed compatibility information, setup videos, and additional support resources, visit the <a href="../../fr.html" target="_self">UA Support Knowledge Base</a>.

The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are now properly initialized and ready for use the next time Pro Tools is opened.

#### Firmware Update Information

- For optimum results, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, visit the [firmware updates support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-windows.html#firmware).

## Version 8.5.1 - February 2, 2016

### About This Software (Mac only)

- This version supports all Apollo audio interfaces using Thunderbolt for the computer connection. If connecting Apollo or Apollo 16 to the computer via FireWire, use the concurrent UAD v8.5.0 release instead.
- This version supports all UAD-2 devices except Apollo models connected via FireWire.

### New UAD Plug-Ins from Direct Development Partners

- [Marshall JMP 2203](http://www.uaudio.com/store/guitar-bass/marshall-jmp2203.html) by Softube
- [Oxford Envolution](http://www.uaudio.com/store/special-processing/oxford-envolution.html) by Sonnox
- [bx_digital V3](http://www.uaudio.com/store/mastering/brainworx-bx-digital3.html) by Brainworx

### Other Changes

- Improved graphical interface and Pro Tools page tables for existing UAD plug-ins: Fairchild 670 Legacy, Neve 1073 Legacy, Neve 1073SE Legacy, Precision K-Stereo
- Compatibility with Mac OS X El Capitan
- Mac OS X Mountain Lion is no longer tested

### Details About This Release

#### Firmware Update Information

- For optimum results, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, visit the [firmware updates support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html#firmware).

#### Mac OS X El Capitan Compatibility

- UAD v8.5 and higher is tested and compatible with Mac OS X 10.11 El Capitan.
- UAD v8.5 is tested and compatible with released versions of Mac OS X 10.9 Mavericks, 10.10 Yosemite, and 10.11 El Capitan. Pre-release and beta OS versions are not supported.
- Mac OS X 10.8 Mountain Lion is no longer tested.

#### Apollo Expanded Information

- Multi-Unit Cascading: Inter-unit wiring is changed with UAD v8. Only a single Thunderbolt cable is needed for each Apollo unit, and no other cables (ADAT, Word Clock, FireWire, MADI) should be connected between Apollo units. See the <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support#multi-unit" target="_self">Apollo Thunderbolt support page</a> or <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/manuals.html" target="_self">Apollo Thunderbolt Software Manual</a> for details.
- Device Compatibility: For detailed device compatibility information related to UAD v8, see the support page for your device: <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support" target="_self">Apollo & Apollo 16</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/apollo-twin-support" target="_self">Apollo Twin</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/pcie-support" target="_self">UAD-2 PCIe</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/satellite-tb-support" target="_self">UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/satellite-support" target="_self">UAD-2 Satellite FireWire</a>

### About Apollo Thunderbolt Software

- This release uses the PCIe protocol via Thunderbolt for all audio I/O stream processing. Because FireWire I/O drivers are not included, Thunderbolt must be used for Apollo’s connection to the computer.
- Important: Apollo Thunderbolt software disables the FireWire ports on Apollo and Apollo 16. After loading the required firmware contained in all [UAD Thunderbolt software](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html#sw):
  - Apollo cannot be connected to the computer via FireWire
  - FireWire devices cannot be connected to the Apollo FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices must be disconnected from Apollo’s FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices may be connected to different FireWire ports, such as a:
    - FireWire port on the Mac (if available)
    - Thunderbolt port via the <a href="http://store.apple.com/us/product/MD464ZM/A?fnode=51" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Apple Thunderbolt to FireWire Adapter</a>
    - Thunderbolt hub that has a FireWire port
- Apollo's firmware can be manually downgraded to reenable FireWire port functionality. For instructions, [click here](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html#downgrade).
- For complete details, see the [Thunderbolt support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support).

## Version 8.5.0 - February 2, 2016

### About This Software

- This version supports all Apollo audio interfaces using FireWire for the computer connection. If connecting Apollo models to the computer via Thunderbolt, use the concurrent UAD v8.5.1 release instead.
- This version supports all UAD-2 devices except UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt, Apollo Twin, and next-gen Apollo models without FireWire ports.

### New UAD Plug-Ins from Direct Development Partners

- [Marshall JMP 2203](http://www.uaudio.com/store/guitar-bass/marshall-jmp2203.html) by Softube
- [Oxford Envolution](http://www.uaudio.com/store/special-processing/oxford-envolution.html) by Sonnox
- [bx_digital V3](http://www.uaudio.com/store/mastering/brainworx-bx-digital3.html) by Brainworx

### Other Changes

- Improved graphical interfaces and Pro Tools page tables for existing UAD plug-ins: Fairchild 670 Legacy, Neve 1073 Legacy, Neve 1073SE Legacy, Precision K-Stereo
- Compatibility with Mac OS X El Capitan
- Mac OS X Mountain Lion is no longer tested

### Details About This Release

#### Firmware Update Information

- For optimum results, always update Universal Audio device firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, visit the firmware updates support page for your platform: [Mac](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html#firmware) \| [Windows](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-windows.html#firmware)

#### Mac OS X El Capitan Compatibility

- UAD v8.5 and higher is tested and compatible with Mac OS X 10.11 El Capitan.
- UAD v8.5 is tested and compatible with released versions of Mac OS X 10.9 Mavericks, 10.10 Yosemite, and 10.11 El Capitan. Pre-release and beta OS versions are not supported.
- Mac OS X 10.8 Mountain Lion is no longer tested.

#### Initializing AAX 64 for Windows 7

- Important: To use Avid Pro Tools 11 or Pro Tools 12 with UAD AAX 64 plug-ins under Windows 7, the following steps are required. The procedure must be performed each time an updated version of UAD software is installed (once for UAD v8.5.0, once for future UAD releases, etc): 1. Install [UAD v8](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/support/uad/downloads.html) software. Be sure to restart the computer after installation. 2. Open the Pro Tools application. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are automatically scanned during launch. 3. Click "No" when Pro Tools displays a message indicating some UAD AAX plug-ins failed to load. This message can be safely dismissed. 4. After all plug-in scans are complete, QUIT Pro Tools. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are now properly initialized and ready for use the next time Pro Tools is opened.

### About Apollo Thunderbolt Software

- Important: Apollo Thunderbolt software disables the FireWire ports on Apollo and Apollo 16. After loading the required firmware contained in all [UAD Thunderbolt software](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html#sw):
  - Apollo cannot be connected to the computer via FireWire
  - FireWire devices cannot be connected to the Apollo FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices must be disconnected from Apollo’s FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices may be connected to different FireWire ports, such as a:

    - Thunderbolt hub that has a FireWire port

#### Simplified UAD Authorization

- As of [UAD v8 software](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/support/uad/downloads.html), UAD authorization is automatic (Internet connection required). When the UAD software is updated, authorization happens in the background when the computer is started and/or when the UAD Meter & Control Panel application is opened.
- It is no longer necessary to manually authorize after updating UAD software; you can begin working immediately.
- After purchasing a UAD plug-in, the UAD software requires manual authorization. The web store guides you through the process.

### About Apollo Thunderbolt Software

- This release uses the PCIe protocol via Thunderbolt for all audio I/O stream processing. Because FireWire I/O drivers are not included, Thunderbolt must be used for Apollo’s connection to the computer.

    - Thunderbolt hub that has a FireWire port

- For optimum results, always update firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process. Be sure to follow the instructions on screen.
- Do not interrupt system power during any firmware update routines.

Driver Error Reporting

- If a UAD driver error is detected during use, a dialog window containing a “Send” button appears. Clicking the button will confidentially collect and transmit UAD driver log information directly to Universal Audio for engineering evaluation to help improve software reliability. Clicking “Dismiss” will not transmit any information.

## Version 8.2.1 - July 1, 2015

### About This Software (Mac only)

- This version supports all Apollo audio interfaces using Thunderbolt for the computer connection. If connecting Apollo or Apollo 16 to the computer via FireWire, use the concurrent UAD v8.2.0 release instead.
- This version supports all UAD-2 devices except Apollo models connected via FireWire.

### New UAD-2 Plug-Ins from Universal Audio

- Free [Precision Mix Rack Collection](http://www.uaudio.com/store/channel-strips/precision-mix-rack.html) featuring four plug-ins:
  - Precision Channel Strip
  - Precision Delay Modulation
  - Precision Delay Modulation Long
  - Precision Reflection Engine
- Note: These plug-ins replace the discontinued EX-1, DM-1, DM-1L, and RS-1 plug-ins that were sub-modules of the original CS-1 plug-in. The original CS-1 plug-in remains unchanged and is still included in UAD v8.2 and higher.

### Other Enhancements

- (Neve 88RS Unison) Front panel meter properly responds to line input gain adjustments
- (Apollo) Console inputs are no longer hidden after updating UAD software
- (Apollo) Firmware improvements for Apollo 8 and Apollo 8p
- (Pro Tools) Corrected ICON control mapping for UA 1176LN Rev E plug-in
- (Steinberg) Nuendo 7 is qualified
- Click "Show More Detail" below for additional information about this release

### Details About This Release

#### About the Precision Mix Rack Collection

- As of UAD v8.2, the Precision Mix Rack Collection plug-ins (Precision Channel Strip, Precision Delay Mod, Precision Delay Mod Long, Precision Reflection Engine) replace the discontinued EX-1, DM-1, DM-1L, and RS-1 plug-ins, respectively.
- When sessions containing the discontinued EX-1, DM-1, DM-1L, and RS-1 plug-ins are loaded in UAD v8.2 (and higher), the discontinued plug-ins, and their settings and presets, are automatically migrated to their newer Precision Mix Rack Collection replacements.
- For additional details about migrating the discontinued plug-ins from earlier UAD versions, see the “CS-1 Channel Strip” chapter in the [UAD Plug-Ins Manual](http://www.uaudio.com/support/manuals.html).
- Complete documentation for all plug-ins in the Precision Mix Rack Collection is available in the [UAD Plug-Ins Manual](http://www.uaudio.com/support/manuals.html).

#### Multi-Unit Cascading with Apollo Expanded

- Inter-unit wiring is changed with UAD v8. Only a single Thunderbolt cable is needed for each Apollo unit, and no other cables (ADAT, Word Clock, FireWire, MADI) should be connected between Apollo units. See the <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support#multi-unit" target="_self">Apollo Thunderbolt support page</a> or <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/manuals.html" target="_self">Apollo Software Manual</a> for details.
