  - Apollo cannot be connected to the computer via FireWire
  - FireWire devices cannot be connected to the Apollo FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices must be disconnected from Apollo’s FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices may be connected to different FireWire ports, such as a:
    - FireWire port on the Mac (if available)
    - Thunderbolt port via the <a href="http://store.apple.com/us/product/MD464ZM/A?fnode=51" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Apple Thunderbolt to FireWire Adapter</a>
    - Thunderbolt hub that has a FireWire port
- Apollo's firmware can be manually downgraded to reenable FireWire port functionality. For instructions, [click here](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html#downgrade).
- For complete details, see the [Thunderbolt support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support).

## Version 8.2.0 - July 1, 2015

### About This Software

- This version supports all Apollo audio interfaces using FireWire for the computer connection. If connecting Apollo models to the computer via Thunderbolt, use the concurrent UAD v8.2.1 release instead.
- This version supports all UAD-2 devices except UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt, Apollo Twin, and next-gen Apollo models without FireWire ports.

### New UAD-2 Plug-Ins from Universal Audio

- Free [Precision Mix Rack Collection](http://www.uaudio.com/store/channel-strips/precision-mix-rack.html) featuring four plug-ins:
  - Precision Channel Strip
  - Precision Delay Modulation
  - Precision Delay Modulation Long
  - Precision Reflection Engine
- Note: These plug-ins replace the discontinued EX-1, DM-1, DM-1L, and RS-1 plug-ins that were sub-modules of the original CS-1 plug-in. The original CS-1 plug-in remains unchanged and is still included in UAD v8.2 and higher.

### Other Enhancements

- (Neve 88RS Unison) Apollo input meter properly responds to line input gain adjustments
- (Neve 88RS Unison) Console sessions properly recall saved Hi-Z gain levels
- (Pro Tools) Corrected ICON control mapping for UA 1176LN Rev E plug-in
- (Steinberg) Nuendo 7 is qualified

### Details About This Release

### About the Precision Mix Rack Collection

- As of UAD v8.2, the Precision Mix Rack Collection plug-ins (Precision Channel Strip, Precision Delay Mod, Precision Delay Mod Long, Precision Reflection Engine) replace the discontinued EX-1, DM-1, DM-1L, and RS-1 plug-ins, respectively.
- When sessions containing the discontinued EX-1, DM-1, DM-1L, and RS-1 plug-ins are loaded in UAD v8.2 (and higher), the discontinued plug-ins, and their settings and presets, are automatically migrated to their newer Precision Mix Rack Collection replacements.
- For additional details about migrating the discontinued plug-ins from earlier UAD versions, see the “CS-1 Channel Strip” chapter in the [UAD Plug-Ins Manual](http://www.uaudio.com/support/manuals.html).
- Complete documentation for all plug-ins in the Precision Mix Rack Collection is available in the [UAD Plug-Ins Manual](http://www.uaudio.com/support/manuals.html).

#### Initializing AAX 64 for Windows 7

- Important: To use Avid Pro Tools 11 or Pro Tools 12 with UAD AAX 64 plug-ins under Windows 7, the following steps are required. The procedure must be performed each time an updated version of UAD software is installed (once for UAD v8.2.0, once for future UAD releases, etc): 1. Install [UAD v8](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/support/uad/downloads.html) software. Be sure to restart the computer after installation. 2. Open the Pro Tools application. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are automatically scanned during launch. 3. Click "No" when Pro Tools displays a message indicating some UAD AAX plug-ins failed to load. This message can be safely dismissed. 4. After all plug-in scans are complete, QUIT Pro Tools. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are now properly initialized and ready for use the next time Pro Tools is opened.

#### UAD session compatibility between Mac and Windows with Pro Tools

- Pro Tools sessions containing UAD plug-ins are cross-platform compatible between Mac and Windows systems when using Pro Tools versions 10.3.10, 11.2, and 12. For complete details, see the [Pro Tools support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility/rtas.html).

#### Simplified UAD Authorization

- As of [UAD software v8](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/support/uad/downloads.html), UAD authorization is automatic (Internet connection required). If the UAD software is updated, authorization happens in the background when the computer is started and/or when the UAD Meter & Control Panel application is opened.
- It is no longer necessary to manually authorize after updating UAD software; you can begin working immediately.
- After purchasing a UAD plug-in, the UAD software requires manual authorization. The web store guides you through the process.

### Firmware Update Information

- For optimum results, always update the firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process. Be sure to follow the instructions on screen.
- Do not interrupt system power during any firmware update routines.

#### Driver Error Reporting

- If a UAD driver error is detected during use, a dialog window containing a “Send” button appears. Clicking the button will confidentially collect and transmit UAD driver log information directly to Universal Audio for engineering evaluation to help improve software reliability. Clicking “Dismiss” will not transmit any information.

## Version 8.1.3 - May 28, 2015

### About This Software (Mac only)

- This version supports all Apollo audio interfaces using Thunderbolt for the computer connection. If connecting Apollo or Apollo 16 to the computer via FireWire, use the concurrent UAD v8.1.2 release instead.
- This version supports all UAD-2 devices except Apollo models connected via FireWire.

#### Changes In This Maintenance Release

- Firmware improvements for Apollo 16 mkII

### Details About This Release

#### Multi-Unit Cascading with Apollo Expanded

- Inter-unit wiring is changed with UAD v8. Only a single Thunderbolt cable is needed for each Apollo unit, and no other cables (ADAT, Word Clock, FireWire, MADI) should be connected between Apollo units. See the <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support#multi-unit" target="_self">Apollo Thunderbolt support page</a> or <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/manuals.html" target="_self">Apollo Software Manual</a> for details.

#### Related Apollo Expanded Information

- For detailed device compatibility information related to UAD v8, see the support page for your device: <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support" target="_self">Apollo & Apollo 16</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/apollo-twin-support" target="_self">Apollo Twin</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/pcie-support" target="_self">UAD-2 PCIe</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/satellite-tb-support" target="_self">UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/satellite-support" target="_self">UAD-2 Satellite FireWire</a>

### Additional Information

#### Apollo Firmware Updates

- This release contains updated firmware for Apollo 16 mkII that improves performance with this model.
- For optimum results, always update the firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process; be sure to follow the instructions on screen. Most importantly, power off then power on the unit after the "Power Off UAD Device" window appears.
- For additional information, visit the [firmware updates support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html#firmware).

#### Simplified UAD Authorization

- As of [UAD v8 software](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/support/uad/downloads.html), UAD authorization is automatic (Internet connection required). When the UAD software is updated, authorization happens in the background when the computer is started and/or when the UAD Meter & Control Panel application is opened.
- It is no longer necessary to manually authorize after updating UAD software; you can begin working immediately.
- After purchasing a UAD plug-in, the UAD software requires manual authorization. The web store guides you through the process.

### About Apollo Thunderbolt Software

- This release uses the PCIe protocol via Thunderbolt for all audio I/O stream processing. Because FireWire I/O drivers are not included, Thunderbolt must be used for Apollo’s connection to the computer.
- Important: Apollo Thunderbolt software disables the FireWire ports on Apollo and Apollo 16. After loading the required firmware contained in all [UAD Thunderbolt software](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html#sw):
  - Apollo cannot be connected to the computer via FireWire
  - FireWire devices cannot be connected to the Apollo FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices must be disconnected from Apollo’s FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices may be connected to different FireWire ports, such as a:
    - FireWire port on the Mac (if available)
    - Thunderbolt port via the <a href="http://store.apple.com/us/product/MD464ZM/A?fnode=51" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Apple Thunderbolt to FireWire Adapter</a>
    - Thunderbolt hub that has a FireWire port
- Apollo's firmware can be manually downgraded to reenable FireWire port functionality. For instructions, [click here](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html#downgrade).
- For complete details, see the [Thunderbolt support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support).

## Version 8.0.1 - March 3, 2015

### About This Software (Mac only)

- This version supports all Apollo audio interfaces using Thunderbolt for the computer connection. If connecting Apollo or Apollo 16 to the computer via FireWire, use the concurrent UAD v8.0.0 release instead.
- This version supports all UAD-2 devices.

### New UAD-2 Plug-Ins from Universal Audio

- Unison-enabled [Distortion Essentials Pedals](http://www.uaudio.com/store/plug-in-bundles/distortion-essentials-bundle.html) featuring:
  - [Ibanez Tube Screamer TS808](http://www.uaudio.com/store/guitar-bass/tube-screamer.html)
  - Bermuda Triangle
  - Raw Distortion

### New UAD-2 Plug-Ins from Direct Development Partners

- [Sound Machine Wood Works](http://www.uaudio.com/store/guitar-bass/sound-machine-wood-works.html) by Sound Machine
- [Friedman Amplifiers Collection](http://www.uaudio.com/store/guitar-bass/friedman-amplifiers-plug-in-collection.html) by Brainworx

### Other Enhancements

- Apollo Expanded, featuring:
  - Mix-and-match compatibility with up to four Apollo interfaces
  - New Console 2.0 application with over 25 new user-requested features
  - Flex Driver enables custom I/O routes and names at the Core Audio driver level
- Compatibility with up to six UA devices
- Simplified UAD authorization (Internet connection required)
- (Apollo) Unison technology for new [Distortion Essentials Pedals](http://www.uaudio.com/store/plug-in-bundles/distortion-essentials-bundle.html)
- (ENGL/Chandler) Optimized PGM resources and faster controls response
- (Mac) Mac OS X Yosemite compatibility
- (Pro Tools) Avid Pro Tools 12 compatibility (UAD v8 required)

### UAD v8.0.1 Release Details

#### System sleep and Thunderbolt device hot-plugging are incompatible with this release

- UAD v8.0.1 is incompatible with system sleep and connecting/disconnecting Thunderbolt devices when the computer is on. This will be improved in a future release.
- Required: Connect and power on all Thunderbolt devices BEFORE powering on (starting) the computer. Disconnect and power off all Thunderbolt devices AFTER shutting down (powering off) the computer.
- To disable system sleep, open the Energy Saver panel within System Preferences and drag the “Computer Sleep” slider to “Never” (far right position).
- Note: If Apollo is disconnected while the computer is on, system sound may no longer be heard. This will be improved in a future release. System sound can be re-enabled by option-clicking the Speaker icon in the Mac OS X Menu Bar (at upper-right of screen) and selecting an output other than Apollo from the "Output Device" list.

#### Apollo Expanded firmware updates require complete system power down

- This release includes firmware updates. After updating the firmware, the computer and all UAD devices must be fully powered down.
- Important: After clicking "Load" to initiate the firmware update(s): 1. Wait for the "Power Down System" dialog 2. Shut down the computer (power OFF) 3. Power OFF all UA devices 4. Power ON all UA devices 5. Start the computer After the above steps are complete, the system is ready for use.

#### Multi-Unit Cascading with Apollo Expanded

- Inter-unit wiring is changed with UAD v8. Only a single Thunderbolt cable is needed for each Apollo unit, and no other cables (ADAT, Word Clock, FireWire, MADI) should be connected between Apollo units. See the <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support#multi-unit" target="_self">Apollo Thunderbolt support page</a> or <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/manuals.html" target="_self">Apollo Software Manual</a> for details.
- External ADAT input can only be routed into an Apollo DUO/QUAD when the Apollo DUO/QUAD is the designated monitor unit (with UAD v7, external ADAT was routed into the expander unit). This will be improved in a future release.
- When more than one Apollo DUO/QUAD is used with Apollo Expanded, ADAT inputs are supported with the monitor unit only. This will be improved in a future release.

#### Related Apollo Expanded Information

- For detailed device compatibility information related to this release, see the support page for your device: <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support" target="_self">Apollo & Apollo 16</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/apollo-twin-support" target="_self">Apollo Twin</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/pcie-support" target="_self">UAD-2 PCIe</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/satellite-tb-support" target="_self">UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt</a> \| <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/satellite-support" target="_self">UAD-2 Satellite FireWire</a>

### Additional Information<span style="font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"></span>

#### <span style="font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;">Simplified UAD Authorization</span>

- As of [UAD v8 software](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/support/uad/downloads.html), UAD authorization is automatic (Internet connection required). When the UAD software is updated, authorization happens in the background when the computer is started and/or when the UAD Meter & Control Panel application is opened.
- It is no longer necessary to manually authorize after updating UAD software; you can begin working immediately.
- After purchasing a UAD plug-in, the UAD software requires manual authorization. The web store guides you through the process.

### About Apollo Thunderbolt Software

- This release uses the PCIe protocol via Thunderbolt for all audio I/O stream processing. Because FireWire I/O drivers are not included, Thunderbolt must be used for Apollo’s connection to the computer.
- Important: Apollo Thunderbolt software disables the FireWire ports on Apollo and Apollo 16. After loading the required firmware contained in all [UAD Thunderbolt software](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html#sw):
  - Apollo cannot be connected to the computer via FireWire
  - FireWire devices cannot be connected to the Apollo FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices must be disconnected from Apollo’s FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite (FireWire model) and other FireWire devices may be connected to different FireWire ports, such as a:
    - FireWire port on the Mac (if available)
    - Thunderbolt port via the <a href="http://store.apple.com/us/product/MD464ZM/A?fnode=51" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Apple Thunderbolt to FireWire Adapter</a>
    - Thunderbolt hub that has a FireWire port
- Apollo's firmware can be manually downgraded to reenable FireWire functionality. For instructions, [click here](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html#downgrade).
- For complete details, see the [Thunderbolt support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support).

### Firmware Update Information

- All [UAD Thunderbolt software](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html#sw) contains a firmware update that is required to enable the Thunderbolt PCIe audio drivers.
- For optimum results, always update the firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process. Be sure to follow the instructions on screen.
- Do not interrupt system power during any firmware update routines.

## Version 8.0.0 - March 3, 2015

### About This Software

- This version supports all Apollo audio interfaces using FireWire for the computer connection. If connecting Apollo or Apollo 16 to the computer via Thunderbolt, use the concurrent UAD v8.0.2 release instead.
- This version supports all UAD-2 devices except UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt.

### New UAD-2 Plug-Ins from Universal Audio

- Unison-enabled [Distortion Essentials Pedals](http://www.uaudio.com/store/plug-in-bundles/distortion-essentials-bundle.html) featuring:
  - [Ibanez Tube Screamer TS808](http://www.uaudio.com/store/guitar-bass/tube-screamer.html)
  - Bermuda Triangle
  - Raw Distortion

### New UAD-2 Plug-Ins from Direct Development Partners

- [Sound Machine Wood Works](http://www.uaudio.com/store/guitar-bass/sound-machine-wood-works.html) by Sound Machine
- [Friedman Amplifiers Collection](http://www.uaudio.com/store/guitar-bass/friedman-amplifiers-plug-in-collection.html) by Brainworx

### Other Enhancements

- Compatibility with up to six UA devices
- Simplified UAD authorization (Internet connection required)
- (Apollo) Unison technology for new [Distortion Essentials Pedals](http://www.uaudio.com/store/plug-in-bundles/distortion-essentials-bundle.html)
- (API Vision) Fixed audio artifact when engaging PAD
- (ENGL/Chandler) Optimized PGM resources and faster controls response
- (Mac) Mac OS X Yosemite compatibility
- (Pro Tools) Avid Pro Tools 12 compatibility (UAD v8 required)

### Details About This Release

#### Simplified UAD Authorization

- As of [UAD software v8](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/support/uad/downloads.html), UAD authorization is automatic (Internet connection required). If the UAD software is updated, authorization happens in the background when the computer is started and/or when the UAD Meter & Control Panel application is opened.
- It is no longer necessary to manually authorize after updating UAD software; you can begin working immediately.
- After purchasing a UAD plug-in, the UAD software requires manual authorization. The web store guides you through the process.

#### Windows 7 Security Dialog

- UAD v8 software has new driver signing certification. To ensure proper functionality when installing the UAD software, tick the "Always trust software from Universal Audio" checkbox and click the "Install" button in the Windows Security dialog that appears during UAD installation.

#### Initializing AAX 64 for Windows 7

- Important: To use Pro Tools 11 or Pro Tools 12 with UAD AAX 64 plug-ins under Windows 7, the following steps are required. The procedure must be performed each time an updated version of UAD software is installed (once for UAD v8.0.0, once for future UAD releases, etc): 1. Install [UAD v8](https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/support/uad/downloads.html) software. Be sure to restart the computer after installation. 2. Open the Pro Tools application. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are automatically scanned during launch. 3. Click "No" when Pro Tools displays a message indicating some UAD AAX plug-ins failed to load. This message can be safely dismissed. 4. After all plug-in scans are complete, QUIT Pro Tools. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are now properly initialized and ready for use the next time Pro Tools is opened.

#### UAD session compatibility between Mac and Windows with Pro Tools

- Pro Tools sessions containing UAD plug-ins are cross-platform compatible between Mac and Windows systems when using Pro Tools versions 10.3.10, 11.2, and 12. For complete details, see the [Pro Tools support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility/rtas.html).

### Firmware Update Information

- For optimum results, always update the firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process. Be sure to follow the instructions on screen.
- Do not interrupt system power during any firmware update routines.

#### Driver Error Reporting

- If a UAD driver error is detected during use, a dialog window containing a “Send” button appears. Clicking the button will confidentially collect and transmit UAD driver log information directly to Universal Audio for engineering evaluation to help improve software reliability. Clicking “Dismiss” will not transmit any information.

## Version 7.11.1 - November 11, 2014

### About This Software (Mac only)

- This version supports all Apollo audio interfaces using Thunderbolt for the computer connection. If connecting Apollo or Apollo 16 to the computer via FireWire, use the concurrent UAD v7.11.0 release instead.
- This version supports all UAD-2 devices.

### New UAD-2 Plug-In from Universal Audio

- [Manley Stereo Variable Mu Limiter Compressor](http://www.uaudio.com/store/compressors-limiters/manley-variable-mu.html)

### New UAD-2 Plug-Ins from Direct Development Partners

- [Vertigo Sound VSC-2 Compressor](http://www.uaudio.com/store/compressors-limiters/vsc-2-compressor.html) by Brainworx
- [Vertigo Sound VSM-3 Mix Satellite](http://www.uaudio.com/store/mastering/vsm-3-mix-satellite.html) by Brainworx
- [MDWEQ5 Parametric Equalizer](http://www.uaudio.com/store/equalizers/massenburg-mdweq5.html) by Massenburg DesignWorks

### Other Changes

- (Apollo) Cubase I/O buffer setting can now exceed 1024 samples
- (Fairchild 670) Previously-saved CAL and OWR settings are now properly recalled
- (UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt) Firmware update improves overall stability

### Details About This Release

#### Session compatibility between Mac and Windows with Pro Tools 11.2

- Pro Tools sessions containing UAD plug-ins are cross-platform compatible between Mac and Windows systems when using Pro Tools version 11.2. For complete details, see the [Pro Tools support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility/rtas.html).

#### Thunderbolt PCIe audio drivers for Apollo and Apollo 16

- This release uses the PCIe protocol via Thunderbolt for all audio I/O stream processing. Because FireWire I/O drivers are not included, Thunderbolt must be used for Apollo’s connection to the computer.
- Important: This feature disables the FireWire ports on Apollo and Apollo 16. After loading the required firmware contained in all [UAD Thunderbolt software](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html#sw):
  - Apollo cannot be connected to the computer via FireWire
  - FireWire devices cannot be connected to the Apollo FireWire ports
  - UAD-2 Satellite and other FireWire devices must be disconnected from Apollo’s FireWire ports
  - When multi-unit cascading, Word Clock must be used for wiring interconnections instead of FireWire
  - UAD-2 Satellite and other FireWire devices may be connected to different FireWire ports, such as a:
    - FireWire port on the Mac (if available)
    - Thunderbolt port via the <a href="http://store.apple.com/us/product/MD464ZM/A?fnode=51" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Apple Thunderbolt to FireWire Adapter</a>
    - Thunderbolt hub that has a FireWire port
- Apollo's firmware can be manually downgraded to reenable FireWire functionality. For instructions, [click here](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html#downgrade).
- For complete details, see the [Thunderbolt support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support).

#### Important Firmware Update Information

- This release contains a firmware update for the new UAD-2 Satellite Thunderbolt that improves overall stability.
- All [UAD Thunderbolt software](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html#sw) contains a firmware update that is required to enable the Thunderbolt PCIe audio drivers.
- For optimum results, always update the firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process. Be sure to follow the instructions on screen.
- Do not interrupt system power during any firmware update routines.

#### Driver Error Reporting

- If a UAD driver error is detected during use, a dialog window containing a “Send” button appears. Clicking the button will confidentially collect and transmit UAD driver log information directly to Universal Audio for engineering evaluation to help improve software reliability. Clicking “Dismiss” will not transmit any information.

- This release uses the PCIe protocol via Thunderbolt for all audio I/O stream processing. - Pro Tools sessions containing UAD plug-ins are cross-platform compatible between Mac and Windows systems when using Pro Tools version 11.2. For complete details, please see the [Pro Tools support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility/rtas.html).

#### Important Firmware Update Information

- For optimum results, always update the firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process. Be sure to follow the instructions on screen.
- Do not interrupt system power during any firmware update routines.

#### Driver Error Reporting

- If a UAD driver error is detected during use, a dialog window containing a new “Send” button appears. Clicking the button will confidentially collect and transmit UAD driver log information directly to Universal Audio for engineering evaluation to help improve software reliability. Clicking the “Dismiss” button will not transmit any information.

## Version 7.7.1 - May 8, 2014

### About This Release (Mac only)

- This release supports all UAD-2 devices.
- This release supports all Apollo audio interfaces using Thunderbolt for the computer connection.
- Important: If connecting Apollo or Apollo 16 to the computer via FireWire, use the concurrent UAD v7.7.0 release.

### New UAD-2 Plug-In from Universal Audio

- <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/store/unison/neve-1073-collection.html" target="_self">Neve 1073 Preamp and EQ Collection</a>

### New Apollo Platform Features

- Neve 1073 Preamp and EQ enabled for Unison Technology
- Console input labeling (“scribble strips”)
- Thunderbolt PCIe audio drivers for Apollo and Apollo 16 Important: This feature disables the FireWire ports on Apollo and Apollo 16
- Apollo Twin compatibility with UAD-2 devices

### Other Changes

- (Pro Tools) Resolved missing control surface layouts issue introduced in UAD v7.6
- Apple Mac Pro (Late 2013) is fully tested with <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility#macpro2013" target="_self">compatible UAD devices</a>

### Details About This Release

#### Thunderbolt PCIe audio drivers for Apollo and Apollo 16

- This release uses the PCIe protocol via Thunderbolt for all audio I/O stream processing. Because FireWire I/O drivers are not included, Thunderbolt must be used for Apollo’s connection to the computer.
- Important: This feature disables the FireWire ports on Apollo and Apollo 16. After loading the required firmware contained in UAD v7.7.1:
  - Apollo cannot be connected to the computer via FireWire.
  - FireWire devices cannot be connected to the Apollo FireWire ports.
  - UAD-2 Satellite and other FireWire devices must be disconnected from Apollo’s FireWire ports.
  - UAD-2 Satellite and other FireWire devices can be connected to different FireWire ports, such as a:
    - FireWire port on the Mac (if available)
    - Thunderbolt port via the <a href="http://store.apple.com/us/product/MD464ZM/A?fnode=51" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Apple Thunderbolt to FireWire Adapter</a>
    - Thunderbolt hub that has a FireWire port
- When multi-unit cascading, Word Clock must be used for wiring interconnections instead of FireWire.
- For complete details, see the [Thunderbolt support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/thunderbolt-support).

#### Important Firmware Update Information

- This software contains a firmware update that is required to enable the Thunderbolt PCIe audio drivers.
- For optimum results, always update the firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process. Be sure to follow the instructions on screen.
- Do not interrupt system power during any firmware update routines.

#### Apollo Twin compatibility with UAD-2 devices

- This release supports the combined operation of Apollo Twin with UAD-2 Satellite and/or UAD-2 PCIe cards.
- UAD-2 PCIe cards can be used via a [compatible Thunderbolt to PCIe chassis](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/pcie-support#thunderbolt).
- UAD-2 Satellite can be used via the <a href="http://store.apple.com/us/product/MD464ZM/A?fnode=51" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Apple Thunderbolt to FireWire Adapter</a>.
- For complete details, see the [Apollo Twin support page](http://www.uaudio.com/support/apollo-twin-support).

#### Software co-install for different Apollo hardware models

- This software can be used with all Apollo interfaces (separate installers for Apollo & Apollo Twin are no longer required).
- Connecting different Apollo hardware models to the computer simultaneously is not currently compatible.
- Console sessions are not interchangeable between different Apollo hardware models.

#### Neve 1073 Legacy plug-in renaming

- The original Neve 1073 and Neve 1073SE plug-ins are renamed to “Neve 1073 Legacy” and “Neve 1073SE Legacy” to improve differentiation between the older and newer models.
- When DAW sessions containing the older plug-ins are loaded, the renamed Legacy plug-ins are loaded automatically, and all previous settings are retained.

#### Driver Error Reporting

- If a UAD driver error is detected during use, a dialog window containing a new “Send” button appears. Clicking the button will confidentially collect and transmit UAD driver log information directly to Universal Audio for engineering evaluation to help improve software reliability. Clicking the “Dismiss” button will not transmit any information.

## Version 7.7.0 - May 8, 2014

### About This Release

- This release supports all UAD-2 devices on Mac and PC.
- This release supports all Apollo audio interfaces using FireWire for the computer connection.
- For all Apollo interfaces that connect to a Mac via Thunderbolt, use the concurrent UAD v7.7.1 release.

### New UAD-2 Plug-In from Universal Audio

- <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/store/unison/neve-1073-collection.html" target="_self">Neve 1073 Preamp and EQ Collection</a>

### New Apollo Platform Features

- Neve 1073 Preamp and EQ enabled for Unison Technology
- Console input labeling (“scribble strips”)

### New AAX Features for Windows 7

- Windows AAX 64 compatibility with Pro Tools 11
- AudioSuite support (offline processing for audio clips)
- Offline bounce support (faster than realtime bounce to disk)
- Multi-mono support (adjust independent settings for multi-channel tracks)
- Important: To use Pro Tools 11 with UAD AAX 64 plug-ins under Windows 7, the following steps are required (once only): 1. Install the UAD v7.7.0 software. Be sure to restart the computer after installation. 2. Open the Pro Tools 11 application. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are automatically scanned during launch. 3. After all plug-in scans are complete, QUIT Pro Tools 11. The UAD AAX 64 plug-ins are now properly initialized and ready for use the next time Pro Tools 11 is opened.

### Other Changes

- (Pro Tools) Resolved missing control surface layouts issue introduced in UAD v7.6
- Apple Mac Pro (Late 2013) is fully tested with <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility#macpro2013" target="_self">compatible UAD devices</a>

### Details About This Release

AAX 64 for Windows 7

- UAD software does not currently provide cross-platform support for AAX 64. Pro Tools 10 and 11 sessions saved under Windows 7 cannot be loaded in Pro Tools 11 under Mac OS X, and vise-versa.

Neve 1073 Legacy plug-in renaming

- The original Neve 1073 and Neve 1073SE plug-ins are renamed to “Neve 1073 Legacy” and “Neve 1073SE Legacy” to improve differentiation between the older and newer models.
- When DAW sessions containing the older plug-ins are loaded, the renamed Legacy plug-ins are loaded automatically, and all previous settings are retained.

Important Firmware Update Information

- For optimum results, always update the firmware by clicking "Load" when prompted by the UAD software.
- The software will guide you through the firmware update process. Be sure to follow the instructions on screen.
- Do not interrupt system power during any firmware update routines.

### Details About This Release

AAX 64 Compatibility

- (Mac) UAD plug-ins for Pro Tools 11 AAX 64 are fully compatible under Mac OS X 10.8 Mountain Lion and 10.9 Mavericks.
- (Win) This release does not include AAX plug-ins. Pro Tools 11 compatibility for Windows 7 is expected in Spring 2014.
- For updated Pro Tools RTAS and AAX information, visit the <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility/rtas.html" target="_self">Pro Tools support page</a>.

Mac AAX changes since UAD v7.4.1 Public Beta:

- Pro Tools 11 Compare function is fully operational
- Optimized operation at high session sample rates in Pro Tools 11
- Settings for UA LA-2A Legacy and UA 1176LN/SE Legacy saved with older UAD versions are correctly recalled
- Settings for Ocean Way Studios saved with UAD v7.4.2 are correctly recalled
- Ocean Way Studios retains mic selections when changing Studio while holding Shift key

Mac OS X Compatibility

- UAD v7.5.0 is tested for compatibility with Mac OS X 10.8 Mountain Lion and 10.9 Mavericks. Although older Mac OS X operating systems may work with UAD v7.5.0, they are untested. For older UAD versions,[click here](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html).
- UAD v7.5.0 does not contain 32-bit device drivers, so it cannot work with discontinued Mac OS X operating systems running in 32-bit kernel mode.
- Mac OS X 10.6 Snow Leopard and 10.7 Lion can run in 32-bit kernel mode or 64-bit kernel mode. For related information and instructions on how to boot in 32-bit vs 64-bit kernel modes with discontinued operating systems, refer to <a href="http://support.apple.com/kb/HT4287" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">this Apple support article</a>.

Important Firmware Update Information

- (Apollo) This release contains firmware for Apollo DUO/QUAD that enables Unison technology.
- (Mac Pro) This release contains firmware for Apollo DUO/QUAD, Apollo 16, and UAD-2 OCTO that enables these devices to be recognized by the new Mac Pro (Late 2013) when connected via Thunderbolt. This firmware has undergone preliminary testing and no issues were exposed, however it is not yet fully tested. Note: The initial firmware update must be performed with a computer other than the new Mac Pro. For complete information and update instructions, <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility#firmware" target="_self">click here</a>.
- For optimum results, always update the firmware by clicking "OK" when prompted by the software.
- After "OK" is clicked and the firmware is installed, a notification appears. After the notification, completely power off the Universal Audio device.
- The first time power is reapplied, the UA device will take an extra 20–30 seconds to initialize, after which the firmware update process is complete.

Important: Do not interrupt system power during any firmware update routines.

## Version 7.4.1 (Public Beta for Mac) - December 10, 2013

### About This Release

- [UAD v7.4.1](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/downloads.html) is a public beta release intended for Mac users running Avid Pro Tools 11.
- This Mac-only release supports all UAD-2 devices (UAD-2 PCIe cards, UAD-2 Satellite, Apollo, and Apollo 16).
- Qualified [host applications](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/host-applications.html) and [operating systems](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility/system-requirements.html) are unchanged since UAD v7.4.0.
- To install UAD AAX 64 support, check the "UAD Powered Plug-Ins for Pro Tools" option during installation. RTAS and AAX 64 plug-ins will both be installed.
- After installing UAD v7.4.1, sessions and presets created in previous versions of Pro Tools can be loaded and used immediately in Pro Tools 11. The transition is seamless.

### New AAX Features (Mac only)

- AAX 64 compatibility with Pro Tools 11
- AudioSuite support (offline processing for audio clips)
- Faster-than-realtime bounce support (offline bounce to disk)
- Multi-mono support (adjust independent settings for multi-channel tracks)

### Other Changes

- Resolved parameter adjustment issues in RealVerb Pro and Dreamverb

### Details About This Release

#### Known AAX 64 Issue

- The Compare function in the Pro Tools preset toolbar (at top of plug-in window) is disabled.

#### Additional Notes

- Complete AAX 64 support, including support for Windows 7, is expected in early 2014.
- For more details about UAD support for AAX 64, please see our <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/blog/support-report-aax-format/" target="_self">Pro Tools AAX Blog</a>.
- Mac OS X 10.9 Mavericks is not fully qualified in this release. For information about Mavericks compatibility, <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility" target="_self">click here</a>.

#### Important Apollo and Apollo 16 Firmware Update Information

- Apollo requires a firmware update to use UAD version 7, and the UAD v7 firmware is incompatible with UAD v6.5.2 and earlier versions of UAD software. The required firmware is in the UAD v7 installer; be sure to click "OK" when prompted by the UAD Meter & Control Panel to update the firmware, then power-cycle (turn off then turn on) Apollo to complete the firmware update.
- If the v7 firmware is used with earlier versions of UAD software, noise blasts and/or fatal DSP errors could occur. If the Apollo firmware is already upgraded to v7 and you wish to use UAD v6.5.2 or earlier versions with Apollo, the firmware must be manually downgraded using the instructions below.

How to downgrade Apollo to version 6 firmware Follow the instructions below to use UAD v6.5.2 (or earlier) software with Apollo if UAD v7 firmware was installed:

1.  Download this firmware binary file for the specific Apollo model: <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/media/support/downloads/Firmware-Apollo-DUO-652.bin" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">DUO</a> \| <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/media/support/downloads/Firmware-Apollo-QUAD-652.bin" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">QUAD</a>
2.  Drag the firmware file onto the UAD v7 Meter & Control Panel application icon to initiate the downgrade. A dialog appears confirming the firmware change.
3.  Click OK to start the firmware change. A confirmation dialog appears after the change is complete, but DO NOT power cycle yet.
4.  Power down Apollo. DO NOT POWER ON.
5.  Uninstall UAD v7 ([Mac](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html) \| [Win](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-windows.html)).
6.  Install [UAD v6.5.2 (or earlier)](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html), then restart the computer.

- After restarting, Apollo can be powered and used with UAD v6.5.2 or earlier. If subsequently upgrading to UAD v7, the v7 firmware must be re-upgraded when prompted (the software and firmware versions must be used together as a set).

### New UAD-2 Plug-Ins from Universal Audio

- (ENGL) Resolved issue where user settings could be incorrectly restored on session recall
- Resolved issue where UAD authorization could be requested twice
- (Fairchild) The original plug-in is renamed to “Fairchild 670 Legacy”

- (Mac) OS X 10.6 Snow Leopard is no longer qualified

### Release Details for UAD v7.4.0

### About Qualified Operating Systems

- Although unqualified operating systems may work, they are not tested and not supported by UA. Prior UAD software for older operating systems and discontinued UAD products is available in the [UAD software archives](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html).
- For information about Mac OS X 10.9 Mavericks compatibility, <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility" target="_self">click here</a>.
- For complete system requirements, <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility/system-requirements.html" target="_self">click here</a>.

### About Legacy plug-in renaming

- Older original UAD plug-ins (1176LN/1176SE, LA2A, Pultec, Pultec-Pro, Fairchild) that are supplanted by newer model plug-ins of the same hardware (UA 1176 Classic Limiter Collection, Teletronix LA-2A Classic Leveler Collection, Pultec Passive EQ Collection, Fairchild Tube Limiter Collection) are appended with “Legacy” in the plug-in name to improve differentiation between the older and newer models and so that they are alphabetically adjacent in plug-in lists.
- When DAW sessions containing the older plug-ins are loaded, the renamed Legacy plug-ins are loaded automatically, and all previous settings are retained.
- (Pultec, Pultec-Pro) These original plug-ins are renamed to “Pultec EQP-1A Legacy” and “Pultec-Pro Legacy”
- (1176LN, 1176SE) These original plug-ins are renamed to “UA 1176LN Legacy” and “UA 1176SE Legacy”
- (LA2A) The original plug-in is renamed to “Teletronix LA-2A Legacy”
- (Fairchild) The original plug-in is renamed to “Fairchild 670 Legacy”

#### Important Apollo and Apollo 16 Firmware Update Information

- Apollo requires a firmware update to use UAD version 7, and the UAD v7 firmware is incompatible with UAD v6.5.2 and earlier versions of UAD software. The required firmware is in the UAD v7 installer; be sure to click "OK" when prompted by the UAD Meter & Control Panel to update the firmware, then power-cycle (turn off then turn on) Apollo to complete the firmware update.
- If the v7 firmware is used with earlier versions of UAD software, noise blasts and/or fatal DSP errors could occur. If the Apollo firmware is already upgraded to v7 and you wish to use UAD v6.5.2 or earlier versions with Apollo, the firmware must be manually downgraded using the instructions below.

How to downgrade Apollo to version 6 firmware Follow the instructions below to use UAD v6.5.2 (or earlier) software with Apollo if UAD v7 firmware was installed:

1.  Download this firmware binary file for the specific Apollo model: <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/media/support/downloads/Firmware-Apollo-DUO-652.bin" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">DUO</a> \| <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/media/support/downloads/Firmware-Apollo-QUAD-652.bin" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">QUAD</a>
2.  Drag the firmware file onto the UAD v7 Meter & Control Panel application icon to initiate the downgrade. A dialog appears confirming the firmware change.
3.  Click OK to start the firmware change. A confirmation dialog appears after the change is complete, but DO NOT power cycle yet.
4.  Power down Apollo. DO NOT POWER ON.
5.  Uninstall UAD v7 ([Mac](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html) \| [Win](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-windows.html)).
6.  Install [UAD v6.5.2 (or earlier)](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html), then restart the computer.

- After restarting, Apollo can be powered and used with UAD v6.5.2 or earlier. If subsequently upgrading to UAD v7, the v7 firmware must be re-upgraded when prompted (the software and firmware versions must be used together as a set).

### New UAD-2 Plug-In from Universal Audio

- [API Vision Channel Strip](http://www.uaudio.com/store/channel-strips/api-vision-channel-strip.html)

### Other Changes

- New <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility/host-applications.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">qualified host</a> applications: <a href="http://www.steinberg.net/en/support/downloads/downloads_cubase_7.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Cubase 7.0.6</a>, <a href="http://www.steinberg.net/en/support/downloads/downloads_nuendo_6.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Nuendo 6.0.6</a>, and <a href="http://www.apple.com/logic-pro/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Logic Pro X</a>
- Mono (m) versions of UAD plug-ins are restored for all titles
- (Oxford EQ) Resolved various stability issues
- (All Amp Room) Enable and stereo states are properly retained
- (Metal Amp Room) Resolved various stability issues
- (Ocean Way Studios) Parameter label corrections for Pro Tools and Avid Artist Series control surfaces
- (Apollo Multi-Unit) Expander unit monitor signal is passed to monitor unit upon computer disconnection
- (Apollo/Apollo 16) This release includes a firmware update for improved operation. Be sure to click "OK" when prompted to update the firmware, then power off and power on the Apollo hardware to complete the firmware update process. See below for details.

Release Details for UAD v7.3.0 Notice for Mac OS X 10.8.5 Mountain Lion Users

- A very small number of UAD / Mac OS X 10.8.5 users have reported issues after installing UAD software on systems running Apple’s Mac OS X 10.8.5 Supplemental Update 1.0.
- It has been determined that these issues only result when the critical “mach_kernel” OS X operating system file, which is exposed by 10.8.5 Supplemental Update 1.0, is missing from the OS prior to UAD installation.
- The UAD v7.3.0b [(and higher)](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/downloads.html) Mac installers check for the existence of this system file prior to UAD installation. If the file is missing, UAD installation cannot proceed until the operating system is recovered using<a href="http://support.apple.com/kb/PH10763" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">these instructions</a>. For additional system recovery information, <a href="http://support.apple.com/kb/HT4718" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">click here</a>.
- Note: Detection of the missing “mach_kernel” file by the UAD installer is the only change in v7.3.0b. The UAD software itself is unchanged from the original release, so there is no need to reinstall if already running v7.3.0.

Important Apollo and Apollo 16 Firmware Update Information

- Apollo requires a firmware update to use UAD version 7, and the UAD v7 firmware is incompatible with UAD v6.5.2 and earlier versions of UAD software. The required firmware is in the UAD v7 installer; be sure to click "OK" when prompted by the UAD Meter & Control Panel to update the firmware, then power-cycle (turn off then turn on) Apollo to complete the firmware update.
- If the v7 firmware is used with earlier versions of UAD software, noise blasts and/or fatal DSP errors could occur. If the Apollo firmware is already upgraded to v7 and you wish to use UAD v6.5.2 or earlier versions with Apollo, the firmware must be manually downgraded using the instructions below.

How to downgrade Apollo to version 6 firmware Follow the instructions below to use UAD v6.5.2 (or earlier) software with Apollo if UAD v7 firmware was installed:

1.  Download this firmware binary file for the specific Apollo model: <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/media/support/downloads/Firmware-Apollo-DUO-652.bin" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">DUO</a> \| <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/media/support/downloads/Firmware-Apollo-QUAD-652.bin" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">QUAD</a>
2.  Drag the firmware file onto the UAD v7 Meter & Control Panel application icon to initiate the downgrade. A dialog appears confirming the firmware change.
3.  Click OK to start the firmware change. A confirmation dialog appears after the change is complete, but DO NOT power cycle yet.
4.  Power down Apollo. DO NOT POWER ON.
5.  Uninstall UAD v7 ([Mac](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html) \| [Win](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-windows.html)).
6.  Install [UAD v6.5.2 (or earlier)](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html), then restart the computer.

- After restarting, Apollo can be powered and used with UAD v6.5.2 or earlier. If subsequently upgrading to UAD v7, the v7 firmware must be re-upgraded when prompted (the software and firmware versions must be used together as a set).

#### Important Apollo and Apollo 16 Firmware Update Information

- UAD v7.1.0 includes a firmware update which enables new Flex Routing functionality in Apollo and Apollo 16. Be sure to click "OK" when prompted to update the firmware, then power off and power on Apollo to complete the firmware update process.

### About Legacy plug-in renaming

- Older UAD plug-ins (1176LN/1176SE, LA2A, Pultec, Pultec-Pro) that are supplanted by newer model plug-ins of the same hardware (UA 1176 Classic Limiter Collection, Teletronix LA-2A Classic Leveler Collection, Pultec Passive EQ Collection) are appended with “Legacy” in the plug-in name to improve differentiation between the older and newer models and so that they are alphabetically adjacent in plug-in lists.
- When DAW sessions containing the older plug-ins are loaded, the renamed Legacy plug-ins are loaded automatically, and all previous settings are retained.
- (Pultec, Pultec-Pro) These original plug-ins are renamed to “Pultec EQP-1A Legacy” and “Pultec-Pro Legacy”
- (1176LN, 1176SE) These original plug-ins are renamed to “UA 1176LN Legacy” and “UA 1176SE Legacy”
- (LA2A) The original plug-in is renamed to “Teletronix LA-2A Legacy”

### About the Apollo version 7 firmware update

- Apollo requires a firmware update to use UAD version 7, and the UAD v7 firmware is incompatible with UAD v6.5.2 and earlier versions of UAD software. The required firmware is in the UAD v7 installer; be sure to click "OK" when prompted by the UAD Meter & Control Panel to update the firmware, then power-cycle (turn off then turn on) Apollo to complete the firmware update.
- If the v7 firmware is used with earlier versions of UAD software, noise blasts and/or fatal DSP errors could occur. If the Apollo firmware is already upgraded to v7 and you wish to use UAD v6.5.2 or earlier versions with Apollo, the firmware must be manually downgraded using the instructions below.

How to downgrade Apollo to version 6 firmware Follow the instructions below to use UAD v6.5.2 (or earlier) software with Apollo if UAD v7 firmware was installed:

1.  Download this firmware binary file for the specific Apollo model: <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/media/support/downloads/Firmware-Apollo-DUO-652.bin" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">DUO</a> \| <a href="https://help.uaudio.com/media/support/downloads/Firmware-Apollo-QUAD-652.bin" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">QUAD</a>
2.  Drag the firmware file onto the UAD v7 Meter & Control Panel application icon to initiate the downgrade. A dialog appears confirming the firmware change.
3.  Click OK to start the firmware change. A confirmation dialog appears after the change is complete, but DO NOT power cycle yet.
4.  Power down Apollo. DO NOT POWER ON.
5.  Uninstall UAD v7 ([Mac](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-mac.html) \| [Win](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/troubleshooting/uninstall-reinstall-windows.html)).
6.  Install [UAD v6.5.2 (or earlier)](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html), then restart the computer.

#### Apollo/Apollo 16 multi-unit cascading

- Specific wiring is required and certain constraints apply when multi-unit cascading. See the <a href="http://www.uaudio.com/support/apollo-support#multi-unit" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">multi-unit cascading section</a> of the Apollo support page for details.
- Combining Apollo with Apollo 16 in one computer system is an unsupported configuration.

About the new Windows installer This release introduces a new UAD installer for the Windows platform. Note it is safe to simply install UAD v7 over prior UAD installations. Changes to the installer include:

- Simplified interface
- Removed installation options (all UAD-2 components are always installed)
- Apollo/Apollo 16 software is installed automatically when the hardware is connected for the first time

### Known Issue with Pro Tools

- Note: This issue is resolved in [UAD v6.5.2 and higher](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/downloads.html).

- Values for certain UAD plug-ins are lost when Pro Tools sessions saved with UAD v6.3.2 (or earlier) are reloaded with UAD versions 6.4.0, 6.4.1, 6.5.0, or 6.5.1.

  Specifically, session settings for the original LA-2A, 1176LN, and 1176SE plug-ins will revert to default values. If the session is saved in this state, customized settings for these plug-ins are permanently lost.

#### Known Issues – Mac and Windows

-  
  -  
    - The demo period for UAD API 560 must be started from within the UAD API 560 plug-in window even if the "UAD API 500 EQ Collection" demo is started from the UAD Meter & Control Panel.
    - Cubase 7 is not yet [qualified](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/compatibility/host-applications.html) with this release

**Note**: Complete qualification of Cubase 7 is planned for a future UAD release.

#### Known Issues – Mac

- (Cubase 32-bit only) When performing audio processing via Audio\>Plug-Ins menu or region editor window, UAD plug-in controls may become unresponsive if the plug-in window is moved. To regain control if this occurs, close the plug-in window then reopen it. This issue is resolved in [UAD v6.5.2 and higher](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/downloads.html).
- (Cubase 32-bit only) When performing audio processing via Audio\>Plug-Ins menu or region editor window with UAD Direct Development Partner plug-ins, the UAD Toolbar cannot be used to load or save UAD presets. UAD presets can be loaded using the up/down arrow buttons in Cubase’s preset management tools instead. This issue does not exist in the 64-bit version of Cubase.

### General Information About This Release

#### (Mac) Audio Units plug-in rescan is required

The UAD Audio Units plug-ins may need to be rescanned before they will be recognized by the host software as 64-bit capable. Follow this procedure to force a rescan of all Audio Units plug-ins for all Audio Units hosts (this procedure is unnecessary if already performed for UAD v6.4.1 public beta):

1.  Install [UAD v6.5.0 software](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/downloads.html) then restart the system.
2.  Quit all Audio Units plug-in host applications.
3.  Delete the Audio Units cache file. The file location is: ~/Library/Caches/com.apple.audiounits.cache (Note that "~" indicates the Library folder at the root of the current user's Home folder, not the Library folder at the root of the hard disk)
4.  Launch the Audio Units host application. The "auval" process will launch and rescan all Audio Units plug-ins automatically.

#### (Mac) Using DAWs in 64-bit mode

To use the 64-bit versions of UAD plug-ins, the host DAW software must be in 64-bit mode. To put Mac applications that support both 32-bit and 64-bit operation into 64-bit mode:

1.  Quit application (if open)
2.  In the OS X Finder, navigate to: /Applications
3.  Single-click the application to select (not open) the file
4.  Select "Get Info" from the File menu
5.  In the Info window, uncheck the "Open in 32-bit mode" option
6.  Close the Info window. The application will open in 64-bit mode the next time it is launched.

#### Windows 7 64-bit UAD plug-in support

- If using a 32-bit version of Cubase/Nuendo, updating to UAD v6.5.0 is not recommended.
- 32-bit editions of Windows 7 are unqualified.
- UAD v6.4.0 (and higher) installs both 32-bit and 64-bit versions of the UAD plug-ins. Although 32-bit or 64-bit UAD plug-ins can be used in different sessions, using both types in the same session is not supported.
- After installing UAD v6.4.0 (or higher), the host DAW may need to be redirected to use the 64-bit versions of the UAD plug-ins which reside in a different directory than the 32-bit versions. After redirecting to the 64-bit directory, the UAD plug-ins may need to be rescanned by the host. The directories to use are: 64-bit UAD plug-ins directory: C:\Program Files\Steinberg\VstPlugins\Powered Plugins\\ 32-bit UAD plug-ins directory: C:\Program Files (x86)\Steinberg\VstPlugins\Powered Plugins\\ Important: To ensure the mono (m) versions of the UAD plug-ins remain accessible, use the VST directories above.

#### Windows 7 support for Apollo and UAD-2 Satellite

- To use Apollo or UAD-2 Satellite with Windows computers, a qualified PCIe-to-FireWire 800 adapter card is required. For the list of qualified adapters, see the product support pages: [Apollo](http://www.uaudio.com/support/apollo-support#win-compatibility) \| [UAD-2 Satellite](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/satellite-support#win-compatibility)
- FireWire device hot-plugging and system sleep are not supported in this release.
- Up to one Apollo and one UAD-2 Satellite, or two UAD-2 Satellites, may be used concurrently in the same Windows system. Multiple Apollo units, or more than two UAD FireWire devices, are not currently supported.
- Daisy-chaining of external FireWire hard drives off of Apollo or UAD-2 Satellite is not supported in this release. See the support pages below for additional information.
- For additional details about using Apollo and UAD-2 Satellite under Windows 7, see the product support pages: [Apollo](http://www.uaudio.com/support/apollo-support) \| [UAD-2 Satellite](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/satellite-support)
- Apollo's Thunderbolt Option Card is supported on Mac systems only.

## Version 6.4.1 - January 3, 2013

### About This Release

- UAD v6.4.1 for Mac OS X is a public beta release intended primarily for Apple Logic Pro 9 64-bit users. Although 32-bit and 64-bit versions of VST and Audio Units plug-ins are included, they are not fully tested with other hosts.
- Users of 32-bit hosts such as Avid Pro Tools and Ableton Live 8 should not install UAD v6.4.1. Instead, [UAD v6.3.2](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/downloads.html) is recommended. Full support for 32-bit and 64-bit hosts will be included in a future release.
- This release supports all UAD-2 devices (UAD-2 PCIe cards, UAD-2 Satellite, and Apollo audio interface).

### New Features

- Mac OS X 64-bit UAD Powered Plug-Ins (VST and Audio Units)

#### System Requirements

- Mac OS X 10.7 Lion or 10.8 Mountain Lion is required
- Mac OS X <a href="http://support.apple.com/kb/HT4287" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">64-bit kernel mode</a> is required

#### Known issues in this release

- (Pro Tools) There is a critical

  ### Known Issue with this release that can cause certain UAD plug-in settings to be lost. The issue is resolved in [UAD v6.5.2 and higher](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/downloads.html).

- System sleep and FireWire device hot-plugging are not supported in this release

- UAD plug-in chaining in Logic Pro is temporarily disabled

- Console's Channel Strip feature is temporarily disabled

#### Audio Units plug-in rescan is required

- The UAD Audio Units plug-ins must be rescanned before they will be recognized by the host software as 64-bit capable. Follow this procedure to force a rescan of all Audio Units plug-ins for all Audio Units hosts:

1.  Install [UAD v6.4.1 public beta software](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/downloads.html) then restart the system.
2.  Quit all Audio Units plug-in host applications.
3.  Delete the Audio Units cache file. The file location is: ~/Library/Caches/com.apple.audiounits.cache (Note that "~" indicates the Library folder at the root of the current user's Home folder, not the Library folder at the root of the hard disk)
4.  Launch the Audio Units host application. The "auval" process will launch and rescan all Audio Units plug-ins automatically.

#### About system requirements

- To use UAD v6.4.1 under Mac OS X 10.7 Lion, the operating system must be in 64-bit kernel mode (10.8 Mountain Lion always runs in 64-bit kernel mode). To determine or change the active kernel mode, see Apple's <a href="http://support.apple.com/kb/HT4287" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">64-bit kernel FAQ</a>.
- Mac OS X 10.6.8 Snow Leopard is not qualified with this release.

#### Using Logic Pro in 64-bit mode

- To use the 64-bit versions of UAD plug-ins, Logic Pro must be in 64-bit mode. To put Logic Pro into 64-bit mode:

1.  Quit Logic Pro (if open)
2.  In a Mac OS Finder window, navigate to: /Applications
3.  Single-click the "Logic Pro" application to select (not open) the file
4.  Select "Get Info" from the File menu
5.  In the Logic Pro Info window, uncheck the "Open in 32-bit mode" option
6.  Close the Info window. Logic Pro will open in 64-bit mode the next time it is launched.

## Version 6.3.2 - November 1, 2012

### New UAD-2 Plug-Ins

- New mastering plug-in: [UAD Precision K-Stereo Ambience Recovery](http://www.uaudio.com/store/mastering/k-stereo-ambience-recovery.html)
- New Direct Development Partner mastering plug-in: [UAD Shadow Hills Mastering Compressor](http://www.uaudio.com/store/mastering/shadow-hills-mastering-compressor.html)

### Other Changes

- Mono VST versions are not included for new UAD plug-ins
- (Mac) UAD icons are not duplicated in OS X Dock
- (Logic) Resolved Audio Units plug-in validation issue under OS X Lion 10.7.5

More Detail for UAD v6.3.2

- Mono VST versions are not included for new UAD plug-ins:

  The monophonic VST versions of UAD plug-ins that can be optionally installed — those with "(m)" in the plug-in name — are no longer developed for new UAD plug-ins. The mono VST versions of prior UAD plug-ins can still be optionally installed for compatibility with older sessions that contain UAD (m) plug-ins.

  Note: The standard VST plug-ins (which support stereo and mono configurations) do not consume more UAD DSP when loaded in supported DAWs that use true-mono processing (Logic Pro, Pro Tools, Cubase, Nuendo). However, some supported DAWs (Live and Sonar) do not use true-mono processing on mono signals.

  Additionally, some UAD plug-ins do not use less DSP even in a true-mono configuration. For details about mono vs. stereo DSP usage, see the<a href="https://help.uaudio.com/hc/en-us/articles/215262223" target="_self">UAD-2 DSP Chart</a>.

However, the JRE is not required to install, or use, UAD Powered Plug-Ins. Therefore, the prompt may be dismissed without consequence, or the JRE may be installed if desired.

## Version 5.9.1 - May 27, 2011

UAD-2:

- (Lexicon 224) Right channel input/output gain values are properly recalled

Mac PowerPC:

- See below for details.

More Detail for UAD v5.9.1:

-  
  - In UAD version 5.9.0, if the “Link” parameter in Lexicon 224 is enabled and the Left/Right gain parameters are not set to the default value when a session or preset is saved, the Left/Right gain values are not properly recalled. This issue is resolved in v5.9.1. **Note:** The Left/Right gain values of existing sessions and presets that were saved with UAD version 5.9.0 are properly recalled when loaded with version 5.9.1.

## Version 5.9.0 - May 5, 2011

UAD-2:

- New plug-in: [UAD Lexicon 224 Classic Digital Reverb](http://www.uaudio.com/store/reverbs/lexicon-224.html)
- Resolved “err−75” issues with certain combinations of plug-ins
- Improved DSP load balancing

UAD-2 Satellite (Mac):

- Resolved compatibility issues with Avid/Digidesign 002 & 003 audio interfaces
- Two units can be used together in a single system
- Resolved various “err−98” issues
- Resolved possible unresponsive state when unit is on at system boot or restart
- Resolved issue requiring specific boot sequence with Avid/Digidesign Mbox 2 Pro

Studer A800:

- Support for ganged preset loads via UAD Toolbar
- Resolved crash issue using ganged controls in some hosts

- Resolved “err-26” DSP load rebalancing errors
- Resolved “err-50” issue when “Limit DSP Load” setting is exceeded

### More Detail for UAD v5.9.0

UAD-2:

- Resolved “err−75” issues with certain combinations of plug-ins: This issue could have occurred when bouncing to disk, loading a session, and/or starting playback.

Studer A800:

- Support for ganged preset loads via UAD Toolbar: If the Studer A800 "Gang Controls" parameter is enabled, and a Studer A800 preset is loaded using the UAD Toolbar (at bottom of the plug-in interface), the settings in the loaded preset is now pushed to all instances of the plug-in.
- Resolved crash issue using ganged controls in some hosts: Hosts that were affected include Image Line FL Studio, Ableton Live, and Steinberg Cubase/Nuendo.

UAD-2 Firmware Update:

- UAD v5.9.0 includes a firmware update that improves stability and performance for all UAD-2 devices.
- The firmware is updated automatically by the UAD installer. If the UAD-2 device is not installed when the UAD installer is run, the firmware will be updated the next time the UAD Meter & Control Panel application is launched and the UAD-2 is installed.
- Be careful not to interrupt power to the computer while the firmware is updating.

Additional Notes:

- The "Home" and "End" keyboard shortcuts have been removed from UAD plug-ins. Depending on the parameter being adjusted with these shortcuts (e.g., gain), extreme volume jumps could have occurred unintentionally.

- (Cooper Time Cube) Mono instances of Cooper Time Cube no longer boosts dry signal by +6 dB. In versions prior to version 5.9.0, when UAD Cooper Time Cube was used in a mono-in/mono-out configuration, the dry signal was +6 dB louder than intended if not set to 100% wet. This anomaly has been resolved in v5.9.0. Note about session compatibility: If a session created in UAD v5.8.1 (and prior) uses Cooper Time Cube in a mono-in/mono-out configuration, and that session is loaded under UAD v5.9.0, the dry volume of the Cooper Time Cube instances will be 6 dB lower if not set to 100% wet.

- As of UAD v5.9.0, documentation for UAD Powered Plug-Ins is installed into a "Documentation" subfolder. All documentation files (except the ReadMe) can be found after v5.9.0 installation in these locations:

  Windows:

  Start Menu\>All Programs\>UAD Powered Plug-Ins\>Documentation Macintosh: Startup Disk/Applications/Powered Plug-Ins Tools/Documentation

## Version 5.8.1 (Mac only) - February 22, 2011

## Version 5.8.0 - December 1, 2010

UAD-2:

- New special processing plug-in: [UAD Studer A800 Multichannel Tape Recorder](http://www.uaudio.com/store/special-processing/studer-a800-tape-recorder.html)
- New channel strip plug-in: [UAD SSL E Series Channel Strip](http://www.uaudio.com/store/channel-strips/ssl-e-series-channel-strip.html)
- New compressor plug-in: [UAD SSL G Series Bus Compressor](http://www.uaudio.com/store/compressors-limiters/ssl-g-series-bus-compressor.html)
