- UAD drivers are now compatible with 64-bit kernel mode
- Mac OS X 10.4 "Tiger" is no longer supported

### More Detail for UAD v5.8.0

About the new UAD SSL E Series Channel Strip and UAD SSL G Series Bus Compressor

- The UAD 4K Channel Strip and UAD 4K Bus Compressor were originally released as emulations of the SSL E Channel Strip and SSL G Bus Compressor. Solid State Logic has since authenticated the plug-ins, and after adding enhancements according to their specifications, they are now officially rebranded and licensed by Universal Audio.
- Although the original UAD 4K Channel Strip and UAD 4K Bus Compressor plug-ins can no longer be purchased, they are still included during installation to retain backwards compatibility with existing sessions.

Mac:

- UAD-2 drivers are now compatible with 64-bit kernel mode. This change enables the use of UAD-2 Powered Plug-Ins when the OS X kernel is running in 64-bit mode (the default mode on the latest Mac Pro systems). Only the UAD-2 drivers are 64-bit; the UAD-2 plug-ins still operate in 32-bit mode. Note there are no 64-bit drivers for UAD-1 devices.
- Mac OS 10.4 "Tiger" is no longer supported as of UAD v5.8.0. Many older operating systems still run with prior UAD versions; see the [UAD Software Archives](http://www.uaudio.com/support/uad/archives.html) for older UAD software and a list of which operating systems they work with.

## Version 5.7.0 - September 23, 2010

All Platforms:

- UAD VCA VU is now officially licensed and renamed to UAD dbx 160\
   

UAD-2:

- New delay plug-in: EP-34 Classic Tape Echo
- Firmware update resolves potential flash memory errors\
   

Win:

- UAD Meter settings are now obeyed under certain DAWs with Vista/Win7
- (RTAS) Manley Massive Passive and Precision Enhancer Hz are now installed on non-english language systems\
   

### More Detail for UAD v5.7.0

Attention Windows 7 & Vista users:

- UAD Meter settings are now obeyed under certain DAWs with Vista/Win7. Due to changes required for this fix, the UAD Meter "Configuration" and "Run On" settings may revert to default values after running the v5.7.0 installer. Please make note of the settings in the Configuration Tab and Plug-in Tab before upgrading to v5.7.0. Additionally, if multiple users are setup under Vista/Win7, please run the installer from within each user account.

UAD VCA VU is now UAD dbx 160

- As of UAD v5.7.0, the prior "UAD VCA VU" compressor plug-in is renamed to "UAD dbx 160." Our classic compressor/limiter plug-in is now officially sanctioned and licensed by dbx®. Please be aware of the following conditions when loading sessions created with UAD v5.6.0 (and earlier).

- VCA VU\>dbx 160 Session Compatibility: There are a few known cases where a host application is relying on the plug-in name rather than its unique software identifier key. In these cases, the host will not be able to find the "new" plug-in in v5.7.0 and use it in sessions created with earlier versions (a workaround is below). These known hosts are: Magix Samplitude, Sony Acid, Sony Vegas, Presonus StudioOne, Steinberg Wavelab, Apple Soundtrack Pro, and BIAS Peak Pro/LE (applies only to Vbox presets). The workaround for these hosts is: 1. Quit the host application. 2. Make a copy of the UAD dbx 160 plugin file/bundle. 3. Rename this copy to "UAD VCA VU" (retain the file extension). 4. Relaunch the host application. You should now have a "dbx 160" plug-in and "VCA VU" plug-in available in the host. 5. Copy settings from the session's active "VCA VU" using the UAD Toolbar (in the UAD plug-in window). 6. Replace the "VCA VU" instance with the "dbx 160". 7. Paste the copied "VCA VU" settings into the "dbx 160" instance. Note: This workaround does not work for Audio Units plug-ins under Presonus StudioOne on Mac. There is currently no known workaround for this host.

- UAD dbx 160 Preset Location: With the renaming of VCA VU to dbx 160, your host application may load/save presets from a different location than was previously used for VCA VU. If you saved VCA VU presets using the UAD Toolbar (at the bottom of the UAD plug-in window), you may want to move any existing presets from the old location to the new "UAD dbx 160" preset folder in the same parent folder: Macintosh: Old path: Macintosh HD/Library/Application Support/Universal Audio/Presets/UAD VCA VU/ New path: Macintosh HD/Library/Application Support/Universal Audio/Presets/UAD dbx 160/

  Windows:

  Old path: C:\Program Files\Universal Audio\Powered Plug-ins\Presets\UAD VCA VU\\ New path: C:\Program Files\Universal Audio\Powered Plug-ins\Presets\UAD dbx 160\\ Note: Your host application likely saves presets in a similar manner and the same preset migration is recommended for wherever those presets are stored (the location varies for each host).

UAD-2 Firmware Update

- The UAD-2 firmware update in UAD v5.7.0 prevents potential errors related to the onboard flash memory. This firmware update is recommended for all UAD-2 users.
- The firmware is updated automatically by the UAD installer. If the UAD-2 is not installed when the UAD installer is run, the firmware will be updated the next time the UAD Meter & Control Panel application is launched and the UAD-2 is installed.
- Be careful not to interrupt power to the computer while the firmware is updating.

(Mac) About 32-bit kernel mode

- The most recent Apple Mac Pro systems (the Mid 2010 "Westmere" models) boot Snow Leopard in 64-bit kernel mode by default, instead of 32-bit kernel mode as in prior models.
- Because the UAD v5.7.0 drivers do not support running under Snow Leopard in 64-bit kernel mode, if booted in default mode, UAD devices will show as "Not Found" when launching the UAD Meter & Control Panel or instantiating UAD Powered Plug-Ins.
- To resolve this issue, simply update to UAD v5.8.0 (or higher), which includes 64-bit UAD drivers.
- If you don't want to update to v5.8.0 or higher, you can boot your system into 32-bit kernel mode by holding down the "3" and "2" number keys on your keyboard when powering up the machine. There is also a more persistent solution by setting the kernel architecture boot flag via the Terminal. See Apple's [knowledge base support document](http://support.apple.com/kb/HT3773) for more details.

## Version 5.6.0 - March 11, 2010

All Platforms:

- Enhanced reverb plug-in: UAD Plate 140 is now UAD EMT 140 with additional controls
- (4K Channel Strip) Minor Q control revisions now better reflect the reference hardware
- (FATSO Sr.) Minor Attack and Release control revisions now better reflect the reference hardware
- (Cooper Time Cube) Coils setting in automation now matches GUI value

UAD-2:

- New EQ plug-ins: UAD Manley Massive Passive & Massive Passive Mastering
- New Precision Series plug-in: UAD Precision Enhancer Hz
- Firmware update resolves reboot and “Error 74” issues

Win:

- UAD-2 Driver enhancements significantly improve host CPU performance and address CPU spiking
- Resolved issue saving custom RTAS presets from within some UAD plug-ins

Mac:

- Apple WaveBurner (v1.6.x) no longer crashes on quit\
   

### More Detail for UAD v5.6.0

UAD Plate 140 is now UAD EMT 140

- As of UAD v5.6.0, the prior "UAD Plate 140" reverb plug-in is renamed to "UAD EMT 140." Our plate reverb plug-in is now officially sanctioned and licensed by EMT Studiotechnik GmbH, and it offers several additional controls over the prior plug-in. Please be aware of the following conditions when loading sessions created with UAD v5.5.0 (and earlier).

- Plate 140 \>EMT 140 Session Compatibility: There are a few known cases where a host application is relying on the plug-in name rather than its unique software identifier key. In these cases, the host will not be able to find the "new" plug-in in v5.6.0 and use it in sessions created with earlier versions (a workaround is below). These known hosts are: Magix Samplitude, Sony Acid, Sony Vegas, Presonus StudioOne, Steinberg Wavelab, Apple Soundtrack Pro, and BIAS Peak Pro/LE (applies only to Vbox presets). The workaround for these hosts is: 1. Quit the host application. 2. Make a copy of the UAD EMT 140 plugin file/bundle. 3. Rename this copy to "UAD Plate 140" (retain the file extension). 4. Relaunch the host application. You should now have a "EMT 140" plug-in and "Plate 140" plug-in available in the host. 5. Copy settings from the session's active "Plate 140" using the UAD Toolbar (in the UAD plug-in window). 6. Replace the "Plate 140" instance with the "EMT 140". 7. Paste the copied "Plate 140" settings into the "EMT 140" instance.\
  **Note:** This workaround does not work for Audio Units plug-ins under Presonus StudioOne on Mac. There is currently no known workaround for this host.

- UAD EMT 140 Preset Location With the renaming of Plate 140 to EMT 140, your host application may load/save presets from a different location than was previously used for Plate 140. If you saved Plate 140 presets using the UAD Toolbar (at the bottom of the UAD plug-in window), you may want to move any existing presets from the old location to the new "UAD EMT 140" preset folder in the same parent folder: Macintosh: Old path: Macintosh HD/Library/Application Support/Universal Audio/Presets/UAD Plate 140/ New path: Macintosh HD/Library/Application Support/Universal Audio/Presets/UAD EMT 140/

  Windows:

  Old path: C:\Program Files\Universal Audio\Powered Plug-ins\Presets\UAD Plate 140\\ New path: C:\Program Files\Universal Audio\Powered Plug-ins\Presets\UAD EMT 140\\ **Note:** Your host application likely saves presets in a similar manner and the same preset migration is recommended for wherever those presets are stored (the location varies for each host).

UAD 4K Channel Strip Q Control Changes

- The UAD 4K Channel Strip in UAD v5.6.0 has minor changes to the taper of its Q controls which more accurately emulate the hardware. Sessions saved under UAD v5.5.0 (and earlier) will load under v5.6.0 with new/correct knob positions, but the processing is not affected and resulting audio will not be different from v5.5.0.

UAD EL7 FATSO Sr. Interface Changes

- The color order of the LEDs for HP Filter, Attack, and Release have been reversed from earlier versions. Existing saved settings/sessions are preserved.
- The 100ms Attack Time label has been changed to 60ms to better reflect actual attack time. Audio processing has not changed, only the interface.
- Minor changes have been made to the Attack and Release compression curves to more closely match the Empirical Labs reference hardware.

Windows UAD-2 Driver improvements

- The "Clear CPU Affinity" setting that was introduced in UAD v5.5.0 has been replaced with "Enable CPU Optimization" (clearing the CPU affinity is no longer necessary with the new option). This new "Enable CPU Optimization" option enables significant UAD-2 driver performance enhancements (reduced host CPU loads and host CPU spiking) for all Windows OS platforms, particularly in cases where a low ASIO buffer size is in use and/or heavy graphics activity.
- This setting is enabled by default, and is recommended for all UAD-2 users running Windows.

UAD-2 Firmware Update

- The UAD-2 firmware update in UAD v5.6.0 ensures the UAD-2 DSP card properly re-initializes itself during a computer reboot/restart. Prior to this firmware update, the UAD-2 may not re-initialize itself during the computer's restart sequence and could result in the hardware not being recognized, or the DSPs crashing on launching of the UAD Meter or UAD plug-ins. This should also resolve cases of DSP Code "Error 74" occurring while using UAD plug-ins. This firmware update is recommended for all UAD-2 users.
- The firmware is updated automatically by the UAD installer. If the UAD-2 is not installed when the UAD installer is run, the firmware will be updated the next time the UAD Meter & Control Panel application is launched and the UAD-2 is installed.
- Be careful not to interrupt power to the computer while the firmware is updating.

### More Detail for UAD v5.5.0

- Important note for RTAS users running Windows Vista: The Mellowmuse ATA v1.4 plug-in for RTAS included in the UAD v5.5.0 installer will not load under Windows Vista, causing an "invalid authorization error" when Pro Tools scans the ATA plug-in. This issue does not occur under Windows XP. If you run RTAS under Vista, we recommend obtaining the currently available ATA plug-in version directly from the[Mellowmuse ATA website](http://www.mellowmuse.com/ATA.html). This issue will be resolved in a future release and we apologize for any inconvenience. The UAD installer overwrites the currently installed ATA version with the 1.4 version. Therefore, install any ATA version other than v1.4 AFTER installing UAD v5.5.0.
- (UAD-2 SOLO/Laptop) UAD v5.5.0 requires a firmware update. The SOLO/Laptop firmware is updated automatically by the UAD v5.5.0 installer. If the SOLO/Laptop is not installed when the UAD installer is run, the firmware will be updated the next time the UAD Meter & Control panel is launched and the SOLO/Laptop is installed. **Note**:Be careful not to interrupt power to the computer while the firmware is updating.
- (Mac) The UAD v5.5.0 firmware enables "Higher Performance" graphics mode support on MacBook Pro "unibody" systems with UAD-2 SOLO/Laptop. Prior UAD versions required "Better battery life" graphics mode. The graphics mode is set in the System Preferences\>Energy Saver pane (this option is not available on all systems).

## Version 5.4.1 - September 3, 2010

UAD-2:

- (FATSO Jr./Sr.) Minor functional and sonic changes improve usability and emulation accuracy:
- All LEDs turn off when power disabled
- Ch 2 parameters default to OFF/"0" in mono instance
- Improvements to interaction between Compressor threshold and Tranny circuit
- Removed discontinuities in the saturation curve at clip level
- Copy+Paste settings from mono to stereo now working
- <span class="bold">IMPORTANT: FATSO Jr./Sr. v5.4.1 session and preset settings are not backwards compatible with v5.4.0</span>

Windows:

- New "Clear CPU Affinity" setting reduces CPU spiking on most multiprocessor systems (UAD-2 only)\
   

### More Detail for UAD v5.4.1

- <span class="bold">IMPORTANT: FATSO Jr./Sr. v5.4.1 session and preset settings are not backwards compatible with v5.4.0. If a session containing UAD FATSO Jr./Sr. is loaded under v5.4.1 and saved, then if the session is reloaded under v5.4.0, the FATSO settings from v5.4.1 will be permanently lost. This applies to FATSO presets as well (there is no way to transfer FATSO settings from v5.4.1 back to v5.4.0).</span>
- (UAD-2 Windows) UAD v5.4.1 introduces the new "Clear CPU Affinity" setting in the UAD Meter & Control Panel "Configuration" pane. Enabling this setting automatically clears processor affinity settings when UAD-2 plug-ins are loaded on multiprocessor systems. This may help reduce CPU overloading and spiking behavior in certain hosts, by forcing UAD-2 plug-ins to run all processors instead of having an "affinity" (preference) for one particular processor. The default value is OFF. If UAD-2 plug-ins are already loaded when the Clear CPU Affinity setting is changed, the host application must be restarted for the change to take effect. Clear CPU Affinity has no effect on single processor systems. If the multiprocessor setting in the host application preferences is disabled then re-enabled, the Clear CPU Affinity setting will no longer have any effect. Therefore, for best results, enable the UAD Meter's Clear CPU Affinity setting AFTER changing the host multiprocessor preference setting.
- (RTAS) UAD v5.4.1 does not include the latest version of the Mellowmuse ATA RTAS plug-in. We recommend downloading and installing the latest ATA version after updating to UAD v5.4.1. The latest ATA version is available [directly from the Mellowmuse website](http://www.mellowmuse.com/ATA.html).

### More Detail for UAD v5.4.0

- (Mac AU) Fairchild Mono has been removed from UAD v5.3.1 (and higher). Loading a session containing Fairchild Mono with UAD v5.4.0 (and higher) will cause a "plug-in not found" error, and the Fairchild Mono settings will be lost if the session is then saved. To convert v5.3.0 (and earlier) sessions that use Fairchild Mono for v5.3.1 and higher compatibility: 1. Install UAD v5.3.0 (or earlier) before opening the session containing UAD Fairchild Mono. 2. For each UAD Fairchild Mono instance, load a regular UAD Fairchild in the same track, group/buss, or output. 3. Use the UAD plug-in toolbar to copy/paste the settings from each Mono instance to its corresponding regular instance. 4. Delete the Fairchild Mono instances. 5. Save the session. The session will now load properly using UAD v5.4.0 and no settings will be lost.\

### More Detail for UAD v5.2.0

- The Authorization process is significantly streamlined as of v5.0.0. Simply click the "Authorize Plug-Ins..." button in the new UAD Meter & Control Panel application "Plug-Ins" pane, then load the downloaded authorization file. See page 27 in the v5.0.0 manual for detailed procedures.

- (UAD-2) LiveTrack processing is not enabled properly in Nuendo/Cubase v2 and v3. After enabling and disabling LiveTrack for a UAD-2 plug-in, you must toggle the Nuendo/Cubase plug-in disable ("Power") button for processing to work again. This is not an issue in Nuendo/Cubase v4.
- (UAD-2 RTAS) Pro Tools LE and HD are not officially supported with the UAD-2 in v5.0.0 due to crash and/or performance issues. If you elect to use the UAD-2 under Pro Tools, select a Hardware Buffer Size setting of no less than 1024 and use as few RTAS Processors as possible (set in Playback Engine settings in Pro Tools).

- (DM-1/L, RS-1) Right Pan value no longer lost when saved with project

Mac:

- Improved DMA engine provides more efficient PCI data transfer resulting in lower host CPU load
- UAD Driver Utility updated to eliminate errors under Mac OS 10.4.3

Windows:

- DirectX is no longer supported\
   

## Version 4.0.0 - October 5, 2005

All Platforms:

- New chorus plug-in: UAD Roland Dimension D
- Tempo Synchronization for CS-1 and Nigel family plug-ins
- (Precision Limiter) Fixed issue which could cause clicks on mixdown in certain hosts
- (Precision EQ) Presets are now saved correctly under all conditions
- (Fairchild) Cubase/Nuendo no longer crashes when read and write automation are simultaneously enabled
- (CS-1/DM-1/DM-1L) Mod type is now restored properly when set to Tri90 or Tri180 in session/preset
- (CS-1 family) Bank support and new default presets
- (Nigel family) New default presets
- (VST) Mono plug-ins are now installed into separate "Mono" subfolder

Mac:

- Fixed drawing problem where knobs sometimes wouldn't draw if editor instantiated partly offscreen
- Installers are now distributed in .zip format
- Control-click ("select" click) on slider now sends current parameter value to host for automation
- (AU) UAD plug-ins now work correctly in Digital Performer when instantiated in mono-in/stereo-out configurations
- (AU) Fixed crash in Digital Performer when deleting/re-instantiating a plug-in with automation data present
- Mac OS 9 is no longer supported

Windows:

- Optimized "Turbo DMA" engine provides full support for the latest multi-processor and multi-core systems, and enhanced performance with FireWire and USB audio interfaces
- Windows 98SE/ME is no longer supported\

- (Precision EQ) Reduced clicks/pops on initial band enable and power switch toggle

- (AU) Resolved touch automation issues
- (AU) UAD DSP resources released during Logic Pro 7.1 bypass & freeze

- (OS X-VST) Mono UAD plug-ins for cross-platform compatibility and complex routings
- (OS 9) Cycling certain plug-in presets no longer causes system freeze\

## Version 3.6.0 - August 31, 2004

- Resolved UI anomaly in DreamVerb when Horseshoe 2 Shape Blend is at 100%

Mac:

- (OS X) Added auto-unload of UAD plug-ins "orphaned" by forced quit, unexpected quit (crash), or improper cleanup by the host application (This was already being done in Windows and Mac OS 9)
- (AU) Parameters with only two states now display their textual values correctly in "generic" views and on external control surfaces
- (AU) UAD plug-ins pass current Apple AU validation tests\
   

## Version 3.5.2 - June 30, 2004

All Platforms:

- Resolved "UAD Not Responding" error when RealVerb-Pro is used with Pultec-Pro
- Added input mute to RealVerb-Pro and DreamVerb to eliminate noise blasts caused by invalid inputs to the plug-ins
- Resolved issue with DreamVerb in mono-in/stereo-out mode (right channel predelay no longer set to 0)
- Resolved RTAS issue with UAD DelayComp ("Plug-ins" parameter now compensates for multiple plug-ins correctly)
- Improved DMA/interrupt handling to enable higher plug-in counts and/or lower host loads on some systems with multiple UAD cards
- Reduced system memory use (may resolve some card initialization errors, e.g. "No system memory resources", "MapRDRAM failed", etc. under Windows, and resolves potential issues initializing multiple cards under Mac OS X 10.2.x)

Mac:

- (OS X) Reduced DSP load during bypass in most hosts
- (OS X) Text entry implemented
- (G5) Improved performance on G5 systems with multiple UAD cards (particularly with FireWire and USB interfaces)
- (AU) Keyboard shortcuts implemented
- (AU) Mono-in/stereo-out mode in Digital Performer reenabled
- (AU ) GUI meters now continue working if multiple instances of a plug-in are instantiated and one is removed
- (MAS) Fairchild settings now restore properly when session is reloaded\

## Version 3.1.0 - June 6, 2003

All Platforms:

- New EQ plug-in: UAD Cambridge EQ
- UAD Cambridge has full-featured 14-day demo and replaces feature-limited version in 3.0
- New 1176SE "Special Edition" plug-in uses very little DSP
- UAD DSP load limiting avoids overloading host system
- LA2A and 1176LN use less DSP and also more accurately model the hardware with certain extreme settings and/or program material
- TrackAdv has new color to easily distinguish it from DelayComp
- Preflex Morph distortion under certain conditions has been fixed
- 1176LN Input knob in All Buttons mode is more accurate (may affect sessions and presets using extreme settings in this mode)
- Nigel ModDelay/Echo parameters are now properly recalled in Logic Audio
- DelayComp no longer causes noise and/or crashes in some hosts during parameter value changes
- Text entry now accepts "," in place of "." for European users

Mac:

- Up to four UAD cards are supported with automatic load balancing
- New control modes: circular (jump), relative circular (grab), and linear (slider)
- New UAD Meter Configuration window
- Plug-in latency is displayed in System Information window
- RealVerb Materials and Shape parameters now accept text entry

Windows:

- \(DX\) UAD plug-ins have significantly less host CPU load
- Drivers now load after reboot when multiple cards installed on some Win2K/XP systems
- \(DX\) Offline processing no longer truncates end of selected region in most hosts
- \(DX\) Offline Processing no longer results in right channel silence
- \(DX\) Additional Pultec delay is now compensated correctly
- Miscellaneous installer fixes\
   

## Version 3.0.1 - February 21, 2003

All Platforms:

- Unnecessary error messages (err=3, err=29, etc) have been eliminated
- Logic 4.x no longer crashes when mono plug-ins are loaded
- Preflex output is now consistent at all sample rates
- Nigel Tremolo module no longer changes mode when Preflex Morph is used
- Installer and uninstaller have been improved

- UAD Meter no longer causes audio dropouts on some systems
- Fixed problems opening/closing mono plug-in editors during automation playback
- UAD plug-ins now use the host knob mode setting

Windows:

- \(DX\) Improved DirectX support
- \(DX\) Added support for additional DirectX host applications, including: Sonic Foundry Sound Forge, Acid, and Vegas
- \(DX\) Many DirectX issues have been resolved\
   

## Version 3.0.0 - February 4, 2003

All Platforms:

- New EQ plug-in: UAD Cambridge Demo
- Mono versions of UAD plug-ins for Logic Audio
- UAD Track Advance plug-in aligns UAD processed audio tracks with MIDI tracks
- Bypassing UAD plug-ins now releases DSP resources
- New Samples parameter in DelayComp and TrackAdv facilitates Pultec compensation
- Direct text entry of parameter values
- New keyboard shortcuts to reset and toggle between saved and edited values
- Up to 32-bit, 192kHz resolution for all UAD plug-ins
- Graphics resource sharing significantly reduces host memory usage and download size
- UAD plug-ins now display information messages if errors occur
- Overall stability is improved
- ModFilter gain no longer drops when knob touched in highpass mode
- Echo Recirculate parameter is now stored when set to Infinite
- LA2A output no longer muted after Bypass\>Suspend\>Enable
- LA2A/1176LN/Pultec processing now begins at start of audio
- 1176LN automation text now matches user interface text
- Fixed all issues related to 96kHz and higher sample rates
- UAD Meter no longer displays version mismatch on errors even if versions are correct
- UAD Meter now displays correct DSP load (under-reported loads are now reported)

Mac:

- (MAS) ModDelay and Echo parameters in Nigel and TremModEcho are now saved

Windows:

- Up to four UAD cards are supported with automatic load balancing
- \(DX\) DirectX support
- UAD CPU limiting disables UAD plug-ins instead of overloading host system
- Mouse scroll wheel support
- New control modes: circular (jump), relative circular (grab), and linear (slider)
- New UAD Meter includes enhanced System Information and Configuration windows
- UAD Meter now remembers ‘Always on top’ setting when reopened
- UAD Meter spacebar no longer activates plug-in disable button
- Wavelab no longer crashes when quit under Windows 98/Me\

## Version 2.0.1

Windows:

- Advanced Multi-Processing support
- Nuendo in-place processing support
- Latency has been optimized and reduced by 128 samples per plug-in, enabling a minimum latency of 128 samples per plug-in
- New UAD Performance Meter options enable fine tuning of UAD configuration parameters including large ASIO buffer size support for Steinberg users. These may also provide greater compatibility with other VST host applications and DirectX systems using the Fxpansion VST adapter
- Deactivation switch in UAD Performance Meter enables temporary disabling of all active Powered Plug-Ins
- New EX-1M plug-in is a monophonic version of EX-1 that enables independent left and right EQ settings in master effects chains and allows Logic Audio users to conserve UAD DSP resources
- New DM-1L plug-in is the DM-1 with available delay times of up to 2400 milliseconds per channel includes a right-delay and left-delay line Ratio Link switch
- New UAD Delay Compensator plug-in allows simplified latency compensation
- VST host knob mode support for circular, relative circular, and linear parameter changes
- Dialog box provides specific information when plug-ins fail to load under certain conditions, such as UAD out of memory, mismatched sample rates, mismatched buffer sizes, or plug-ins in use by another application
- All-new installer minimizes user intervention required on the various Windows platforms
- Async Distortion problem has been fixed
- CPU host load has been optimized
- Vintage compressor no longer clicks at start of audio regions in Logic Audio
- Vintage compressors 96K operation problems fixed
- Fixed Cubase hang problem on session open/close with stereo Powered Plug-Ins (Disable/Enable Audio workaround for Cubase users should no longer be necessary)
- Fixed Cubase hang problem on file audition in sessions with stereo Powered Plug-Ins
- When insert effects are deactivated with the UAD Performance Meter disable switch, audio is no longer delayed.
- When master effects are deactivated with the UAD Performance Meter disable switch, audio is no longer muted.
- DM-1 disable switch no longer disables multiple instances
- Small one pixel black dots following some knobs and meters have been cleaned up
- CS-1 title panel eliminated; its presets panel is now visible at 1024x768 within Logic
- Title panels have been modified and now use less screen real estate
- RealVerb Pro presets names are now displayed correctly
- Full support of Windows 98/ME/2000/XP operating systems
- Wavelab 3.0 support
- Windows 2000/XP plug-and-play errors fixed
